March 13, 2026

SaPaVe: Towards Active Perception and Manipulation in Vision-Language-Action Models for Robotics

Abstract (English): Active perception and manipulation are crucial for robots to interact with complex scenes. Existing methods struggle to unify semantic-driven active perception with robust, viewpoint-invariant execution. We propose SaPaVe, an end-to-end framework that jointly learns these capabilities in a data-efficient manner. Our approach decouples camera and manipulation actions rather than placing them in a shared action space, and follows a bottom-up training strategy: we first train semantic camera control on a large-scale dataset, then jointly optimize both action types using hybrid data. To support this framework, we introduce ActiveViewPose-200K, a dataset of 200k image-language-camera movement pairs for semantic camera movement learning, and a 3D geometry-aware module that improves execution robustness under dynamic viewpoints. We also present ActiveManip-Bench, the first benchmark for evaluating active manipulation beyond fixed-view settings. Extensive experiments in both simulation and real-world environments show that SaPaVe outperforms recent vision-language-action models such as GR00T N1 and \(π_0\), achieving up to 31.25\% higher success rates in real-world tasks. These results show that tightly coupled perception and execution, when trained with decoupled yet coordinated strategies, enable efficient and generalizable active manipulation. Project page: https://lmzpai.github.io/SaPaVe

摘要（中文）: 主动感知和操作对于机器人与复杂场景交互至关重要。现有方法难以统一语义驱动的主动感知与稳健的、视角不变的执行。我们提出了 SaPaVe，一个端到端框架，以数据高效的方式联合学习这些能力。我们的方法将相机和操作动作解耦，而不是将它们放置在一个共享的动作空间中，并遵循自底向上的训练策略：我们首先在一个大规模数据集上训练语义相机控制，然后使用混合数据联合优化两种动作类型。为了支持这个框架，我们引入了 ActiveViewPose-200K，一个包含 20 万图像-语言-相机运动对的数据集，用于语义相机运动学习，以及一个 3D 几何感知模块，以提高动态视角下的执行鲁棒性。我们还提出了 ActiveManip-Bench，这是第一个用于评估超越固定视角设置的主动操作的基准。在模拟和真实环境中的大量实验表明，SaPaVe 优于最近的视觉-语言-动作模型，如 GR00T N1 和 \(π_0\)，在现实世界任务中成功率提高了高达 31.25%。这些结果表明，当采用解耦但协调的策略进行训练时，紧密耦合的感知和执行能够实现高效且可泛化的主动操作。项目主页：https://lmzpai.github.io/SaPaVe

TLDR: The paper introduces SaPaVe, an end-to-end framework that improves robotic active perception and manipulation by decoupling camera and manipulation actions, and a bottom-up training strategy, with a new dataset and benchmark for evaluation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SaPaVe，一种端到端的框架，通过解耦相机和操纵动作以及自下而上的训练策略来改进机器人主动感知和操纵，并提供了一个新的数据集和基准用于评估。

Authors: Mengzhen Liu, Enshen Zhou, Cheng Chi, Yi Han, Shanyu Rong, Liming Chen, Pengwei Wang, Zhongyuan Wang, Shanghang Zhang

RADAR: Closed-Loop Robotic Data Generation via Semantic Planning and Autonomous Causal Environment Reset

Abstract (English): The acquisition of large-scale physical interaction data, a critical prerequisite for modern robot learning, is severely bottlenecked by the prohibitive cost and scalability limits of human-in-the-loop collection paradigms. To break this barrier, we introduce Robust Autonomous Data Acquisition for Robotics (RADAR), a fully autonomous, closed-loop data generation engine that completely removes human intervention from the collection cycle. RADAR elegantly divides the cognitive load into a four-module pipeline. Anchored by 2-5 3D human demonstrations as geometric priors, a Vision-Language Model first orchestrates scene-relevant task generation via precise semantic object grounding and skill retrieval. Next, a Graph Neural Network policy translates these subtasks into physical actions via in-context imitation learning. Following execution, the VLM performs automated success evaluation using a structured Visual Question Answering pipeline. Finally, to shatter the bottleneck of manual resets, a Finite State Machine orchestrates an autonomous environment reset and asymmetric data routing mechanism. Driven by simultaneous forward-reverse planning with a strict Last-In, First-Out causal sequence, the system seamlessly restores unstructured workspaces and robustly recovers from execution failures. This continuous brain-cerebellum synergy transforms data collection into a self-sustaining process. Extensive evaluations highlight RADAR's exceptional versatility. In simulation, our framework achieves up to 90% success rates on complex, long-horizon tasks, effortlessly solving challenges where traditional baselines plummet to near-zero performance. In real-world deployments, the system reliably executes diverse, contact-rich skills (e.g., deformable object manipulation) via few-shot adaptation without domain-specific fine-tuning, providing a highly scalable paradigm for robotic data acquisition.

摘要（中文）: 大规模物理交互数据的获取是现代机器人学习的关键先决条件，但其严重受限于人工参与数据收集范式的过高成本和可扩展性局限。为了打破这一障碍，我们引入了用于机器人的鲁棒自主数据获取系统 (RADAR)，这是一个完全自主的闭环数据生成引擎，彻底消除了数据收集周期中的人为干预。RADAR 将认知负荷巧妙地划分为一个四模块管道。以 2-5 个 3D 人类演示作为几何先验，视觉-语言模型首先通过精确的语义对象定位和技能检索来协调场景相关的任务生成。接下来，图神经网络 (GNN) 策略通过上下文模仿学习将这些子任务转化为物理动作。执行后，视觉-语言模型利用结构化的视觉问答管道执行自动成功评估。最后，为了打破手动重置的瓶颈，有限状态机 (FSM) 协调自主环境重置和非对称数据路由机制。通过严格的后进先出 (LIFO) 因果序列进行同步正向-反向规划驱动，该系统能够无缝恢复非结构化工作空间并从执行故障中稳健恢复。这种持续的脑-小脑协同作用将数据收集转化为一个自我维持的过程。广泛的评估突出了 RADAR 的卓越通用性。在模拟中，我们的框架在复杂的长时程任务上达到了高达 90% 的成功率，轻松解决了传统基线方法性能骤降至接近零的情况。在真实世界的部署中，该系统通过少样本自适应可靠地执行各种接触丰富的技能（例如，可变形物体操作），而无需特定领域的微调，从而为机器人数据获取提供了一种高度可扩展的范式。

TLDR: The paper introduces RADAR, a fully autonomous, closed-loop robotic data generation system that uses a combination of VLMs, GNNs, and FSMs to generate data for robot learning by planning, execution, evaluation, and environment reset, demonstrated in simulation and the real world.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RADAR，一个完全自主的闭环机器人数据生成系统，它结合使用视觉-语言模型（VLMs）、图神经网络（GNNs）和有限状态机（FSMs）来生成机器人学习的数据，通过规划、执行、评估和环境重置，并在仿真和现实世界中进行了演示。

Authors: Yongzhong Wang, Keyu Zhu, Yong Zhong, Liqiong Wang, Jinyu Yang, Feng Zheng

Simple Recipe Works: Vision-Language-Action Models are Natural Continual Learners with Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL) for Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models is a promising direction toward self-improving embodied agents that can adapt in openended, evolving environments. However, conventional wisdom from continual learning suggests that naive Sequential Fine-Tuning (Seq. FT) leads to catastrophic forgetting, necessitating complex CRL strategies. In this work, we take a step back and conduct a systematic study of CRL for large pretrained VLAs across three models and five challenging lifelong RL benchmarks. We find that, contrary to established belief, simple Seq. FT with low-rank adaptation (LoRA) is remarkably strong: it achieves high plasticity, exhibits little to no forgetting, and retains strong zero-shot generalization, frequently outperforming more sophisticated CRL methods. Through detailed analysis, we show that this robustness arises from a synergy between the large pretrained model, parameter-efficient adaptation, and on-policy RL. Together, these components reshape the stability-plasticity trade-off, making continual adaptation both stable and scalable. Our results position Sequential Fine-Tuning as a powerful method for continual RL with VLAs and provide new insights into lifelong learning in the large model era. Code is available at github.com/UT-Austin-RobIn/continual-vla-rl.

摘要（中文）: 用于视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型的持续强化学习(CRL)是实现能够适应开放式、不断发展的环境的自我提升具身智能体的一个有前景的方向。然而，来自持续学习的传统观点认为，朴素的序列微调(Seq. FT)会导致灾难性遗忘，因此需要复杂的CRL策略。在这项工作中，我们退一步，对大型预训练VLA模型在三个模型和五个具有挑战性的终身RL基准测试中的CRL进行了系统研究。我们发现，与既定认知相反，采用低秩适配(LoRA)的简单序列微调异常强大：它实现了高度的可塑性，几乎没有遗忘现象，并保留了强大的零样本泛化能力，经常优于更复杂的CRL方法。通过详细的分析，我们表明这种鲁棒性源于大型预训练模型、参数高效适配和在策略RL之间的协同作用。这些组件共同重塑了稳定性-可塑性权衡，使得持续适配既稳定又可扩展。我们的结果将序列微调定位为一种强大的VLA模型持续强化学习方法，并为大型模型时代的终身学习提供了新的见解。代码可在github.com/UT-Austin-RobIn/continual-vla-rl获取。

TLDR: This paper demonstrates that simple sequential fine-tuning with LoRA is surprisingly effective for continual reinforcement learning with vision-language-action models, outperforming more complex continual learning strategies.

简要说明: 该论文表明，对于视觉-语言-动作模型的持续强化学习，使用LoRA的简单序列微调非常有效，胜过更复杂的持续学习策略。

Authors: Jiaheng Hu, Jay Shim, Chen Tang, Yoonchang Sung, Bo Liu, Peter Stone, Roberto Martin-Martin

MANSION: Multi-floor lANguage-to-3D Scene generatIOn for loNg-horizon tasks

Abstract (English): Real-world robotic tasks are long-horizon and often span multiple floors, demanding rich spatial reasoning. However, existing embodied benchmarks are largely confined to single-floor in-house environments, failing to reflect the complexity of real-world tasks. We introduce MANSION, the first language-driven framework for generating building-scale, multi-floor 3D environments. Being aware of vertical structural constraints, MANSION generates realistic, navigable whole-building structures with diverse, human-friendly scenes, enabling the development and evaluation of cross-floor long-horizon tasks. Building on this framework, we release MansionWorld, a dataset of over 1,000 diverse buildings ranging from hospitals to offices, alongside a Task-Semantic Scene Editing Agent that customizes these environments using open-vocabulary commands to meet specific user needs. Benchmarking reveals that state-of-the-art agents degrade sharply in our settings, establishing MANSION as a critical testbed for the next generation of spatial reasoning and planning.

摘要（中文）: 现实世界的机器人任务通常是长时程的，且经常跨越多个楼层，需要丰富的空间推理能力。然而，现有的具身基准测试主要局限于单层室内环境，无法反映现实世界任务的复杂性。我们引入 MANSION，首个用于生成建筑尺度、多楼层 3D 环境的语言驱动框架。通过感知垂直结构约束，MANSION 生成逼真、可导航的完整建筑结构，并具有多样化、人性化的场景，从而能够开发和评估跨楼层的长时程任务。基于此框架，我们发布了 MansionWorld，一个包含超过 1000 个多样化建筑的数据集，涵盖医院到办公室等类型，同时发布了一个任务语义场景编辑代理，该代理利用开放词汇命令来定制这些环境，以满足特定的用户需求。基准测试表明，最先进的代理在我们的设置中性能急剧下降，这证实了 MANSION 作为下一代空间推理和规划的关键测试平台地位。

TLDR: The paper introduces MANSION, a framework and dataset (MansionWorld) for generating multi-floor 3D environments from language, designed for training and evaluating robotic agents on long-horizon tasks and spatial reasoning. The framework allows scene editing for specific user needs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了MANSION，一个用于从语言生成多层3D环境的框架和数据集（MansionWorld），专为训练和评估机器人在长程任务和空间推理方面的能力而设计。该框架允许对场景进行编辑，以满足特定用户需求。

Authors: Lirong Che, Shuo Wen, Shan Huang, Chuang Wang, Yuzhe Yang, Gregory Dudek, Xueqian Wang, Jian Su

Enhancing Lightweight Vision Language Models through Group Competitive Learning for Socially Compliant Navigation

Abstract (English): Social robot navigation requires a sophisticated integration of scene semantics and human social norms. Scaling up Vision Language Models (VLMs) generally improves reasoning and decision-making capabilities for socially compliant navigation. However, increased model size incurs substantial computational overhead, limiting suitability for real-time robotic deployment. Conversely, lightweight VLMs enable efficient inference but often exhibit weaker reasoning and decision-making performance in socially complex environments. Achieving both strong reasoning ability and efficiency remains an open challenge. To bridge this gap, we propose Group Competitive Learning (GCL), a strategy designed to amplify the capabilities of lightweight VLMs. Our strategy introduces the Group Competitive Objective (GCO) to harmonize global semantics with distributional regularization, alongside Asymmetric Group Optimization (AGO) to explore the upper limits of model performance. Empirical evaluations on social navigation benchmarks demonstrate that GCL significantly elevates VLM performance. Specifically, GCL enables the Qwen2.5-VL-3B learner model and guide Qwen3-VL-4B to achieve an F1 score of 0.968 and 0.914, representing 40\% and 12\% improvement over vanilla supervised fine-tuning (SFT). Notably, under vanilla SFT, the 3B model initially trails the 8B model (F1: 0.692 vs. 0.755). However, through the GCL, the 3B model outperforms (28\%) the 8B baseline model. These results suggest that GCL provides an effective solution for achieving both high accuracy and computational efficiency in real-world deployment.

摘要（中文）: 社交机器人导航需要对场景语义和人类社会规范进行复杂的融合。 扩大视觉语言模型（VLMs）的规模通常会提高社会合规导航的推理和决策能力。 然而，模型尺寸的增加会导致大量的计算开销，限制了其在实时机器人部署中的适用性。 相反，轻量级VLMs能够实现高效的推理，但在社交复杂的环境中，通常表现出较弱的推理和决策性能。 如何同时实现强大的推理能力和效率仍然是一个开放的挑战。 为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了一种名为群体竞争学习（GCL）的策略，旨在增强轻量级VLMs的能力。 我们的策略引入了群体竞争目标（GCO）来协调全局语义和分布正则化，同时引入非对称群体优化（AGO）来探索模型性能的上限。 在社交导航基准测试中的经验评估表明，GCL显著提升了VLMs的性能。 具体而言，GCL使Qwen2.5-VL-3B学习器模型和Qwen3-VL-4B引导模型实现了0.968和0.914的F1分数，分别比原始的监督微调（SFT）提高了40\%和12\%。 值得注意的是，在原始SFT下，3B模型最初落后于8B模型（F1：0.692 vs. 0.755）。 然而，通过GCL，3B模型的性能优于（28％）8B基线模型。 这些结果表明，GCL为在实际部署中实现高精度和计算效率提供了一种有效的解决方案。

TLDR: This paper introduces Group Competitive Learning (GCL) to significantly improve the performance of lightweight Vision Language Models (VLMs) for socially compliant robot navigation, achieving superior results compared to vanilla fine-tuning and even outperforming larger models.

简要说明: 本文提出了组竞争学习（GCL），旨在显著提高轻量级视觉语言模型（VLMs）在社会适应性机器人导航中的性能。实验结果表明GCL优于传统的微调方法，甚至超过了更大的模型。

Authors: Xinyu Zhang, Atsushi Konno, Toshihiko Yamasaki, Ling Xiao

LABSHIELD: A Multimodal Benchmark for Safety-Critical Reasoning and Planning in Scientific Laboratories

Abstract (English): Artificial intelligence is increasingly catalyzing scientific automation, with multimodal large language model (MLLM) agents evolving from lab assistants into self-driving lab operators. This transition imposes stringent safety requirements on laboratory environments, where fragile glassware, hazardous substances, and high-precision laboratory equipment render planning errors or misinterpreted risks potentially irreversible. However, the safety awareness and decision-making reliability of embodied agents in such high-stakes settings remain insufficiently defined and evaluated. To bridge this gap, we introduce LABSHIELD, a realistic multi-view benchmark designed to assess MLLMs in hazard identification and safety-critical reasoning. Grounded in U.S. Occupational Safety and Health Administration (OSHA) standards and the Globally Harmonized System (GHS), LABSHIELD establishes a rigorous safety taxonomy spanning 164 operational tasks with diverse manipulation complexities and risk profiles. We evaluate 20 proprietary models, 9 open-source models, and 3 embodied models under a dual-track evaluation framework. Our results reveal a systematic gap between general-domain MCQ accuracy and Semi-open QA safety performance, with models exhibiting an average drop of 32.0% in professional laboratory scenarios, particularly in hazard interpretation and safety-aware planning. These findings underscore the urgent necessity for safety-centric reasoning frameworks to ensure reliable autonomous scientific experimentation in embodied laboratory contexts. The full dataset will be released soon.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能正日益催化科学自动化，而多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）智能体正从实验室助理演变为自动驾驶实验室操作员。这一转变对实验室环境提出了严格的安全要求，其中易碎的玻璃器皿、危险物质和高精度实验室设备使得规划错误或误解的风险可能导致不可逆转的后果。然而，具身智能体在这种高风险环境中的安全意识和决策可靠性仍然没有得到充分的定义和评估。为了弥合这一差距，我们推出了 LABSHIELD，一个现实的多视角基准，旨在评估 MLLM 在危害识别和安全关键推理方面的能力。LABSHIELD 基于美国职业安全与健康管理局（OSHA）标准和全球化学品统一分类和标签制度（GHS），建立了一个严格的安全分类体系，涵盖164个具有不同操作复杂性和风险概况的操作任务。我们在双轨评估框架下评估了 20 个专有模型、9 个开源模型和 3 个具身模型。我们的结果揭示了通用领域多项选择题准确率和半开放式问答安全性能之间的系统性差距，模型在专业实验室场景中的表现平均下降了 32.0%，尤其是在危害解释和安全意识规划方面。这些发现强调了迫切需要以安全为中心的推理框架，以确保在具身实验室环境中进行可靠的自主科学实验。完整数据集即将发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces LABSHIELD, a novel multimodal benchmark to evaluate safety-critical reasoning and planning capabilities of MLLMs in realistic scientific laboratory settings, revealing a significant performance gap in professional lab scenarios compared to general-domain tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了LABSHIELD，这是一个新的多模态基准，用于评估MLLM在实际科学实验室环境中进行安全关键推理和规划的能力，揭示了在专业实验室场景中与通用领域任务相比，性能存在显著差距。

Authors: Qianpu Sun, Xiaowei Chi, Yuhan Rui, Ying Li, Kuangzhi Ge, Jiajun Li, Sirui Han, Shanghang Zhang

OmniStream: Mastering Perception, Reconstruction and Action in Continuous Streams

Abstract (English): Modern visual agents require representations that are general, causal, and physically structured to operate in real-time streaming environments. However, current vision foundation models remain fragmented, specializing narrowly in image semantic perception, offline temporal modeling, or spatial geometry. This paper introduces OmniStream, a unified streaming visual backbone that effectively perceives, reconstructs, and acts from diverse visual inputs. By incorporating causal spatiotemporal attention and 3D rotary positional embeddings (3D-RoPE), our model supports efficient, frame-by-frame online processing of video streams via a persistent KV-cache. We pre-train OmniStream using a synergistic multi-task framework coupling static and temporal representation learning, streaming geometric reconstruction, and vision-language alignment on 29 datasets. Extensive evaluations show that, even with a strictly frozen backbone, OmniStream achieves consistently competitive performance with specialized experts across image and video probing, streaming geometric reconstruction, complex video and spatial reasoning, as well as robotic manipulation (unseen at training). Rather than pursuing benchmark-specific dominance, our work demonstrates the viability of training a single, versatile vision backbone that generalizes across semantic, spatial, and temporal reasoning, i.e., a more meaningful step toward general-purpose visual understanding for interactive and embodied agents.

摘要（中文）: 现代视觉智能体需要在实时流环境中运行，因此需要通用、因果且具有物理结构化的表示。然而，目前的视觉基础模型仍然分散，狭隘地专注于图像语义感知、离线时间建模或空间几何。本文介绍了一种统一的流式视觉主干网络 OmniStream，它能够从各种视觉输入中有效地感知、重建和执行动作。通过结合因果时空注意力机制和3D旋转位置嵌入（3D-RoPE），我们的模型能够利用持久的KV缓存，高效地逐帧在线处理视频流。我们使用协同多任务框架预训练 OmniStream，该框架在29个数据集上耦合了静态和时间表示学习、流式几何重建以及视觉-语言对齐。大量的评估表明，即使使用严格冻结的主干网络，OmniStream 在图像和视频探测、流式几何重建、复杂的视频和空间推理以及机器人操作（训练期间未见过）方面，也能够与专门的专家模型达到具有竞争力的性能。我们的工作并非追求特定基准的优势，而是证明了训练一个单一的、通用的视觉主干网络的可行性，该网络可以在语义、空间和时间推理上进行泛化，这朝着交互式和具身智能体的通用视觉理解迈出了更有意义的一步。

TLDR: OmniStream is a unified visual backbone for perception, reconstruction, and action in streaming video, pre-trained on a diverse set of tasks and achieving competitive results across various domains even with a frozen backbone.

简要说明: OmniStream是一个统一的视觉骨干网络，用于流式视频中的感知、重建和动作。它经过了大量任务的预训练，即使使用冻结的骨干网络，也能在各个领域取得有竞争力的成果。

Authors: Yibin Yan, Jilan Xu, Shangzhe Di, Haoning Wu, Weidi Xie

HATS: Hardness-Aware Trajectory Synthesis for GUI Agents

Abstract (English): Graphical user interface (GUI) agents powered by large vision-language models (VLMs) have shown remarkable potential in automating digital tasks, highlighting the need for high-quality trajectory data to support effective agent training. Yet existing trajectory synthesis pipelines often yield agents that fail to generalize beyond simple interactions. We identify this limitation as stemming from the neglect of semantically ambiguous actions, whose meanings are context-dependent, sequentially dependent, or visually ambiguous. Such actions are crucial for real-world robustness but are under-represented and poorly processed in current datasets, leading to semantic misalignment between task instructions and execution. To address these issues, we propose HATS, a Hardness-Aware Trajectory Synthesis framework designed to mitigate the impact of semantic ambiguity. We define hardness as the degree of semantic ambiguity associated with an action and develop two complementary modules: (1) hardness-driven exploration, which guides data collection toward ambiguous yet informative interactions, and (2) alignment-guided refinement, which iteratively validates and repairs instruction-execution alignment. The two modules operate in a closed loop: exploration supplies refinement with challenging trajectories, while refinement feedback updates the hardness signal to guide future exploration. Extensive experiments show that agents trained with HATS consistently outperform state-of-the-art baselines across benchmark GUI environments.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 由大型视觉-语言模型（VLMs）驱动的图形用户界面（GUI）智能体在自动化数字任务方面展现出卓越的潜力，突显了高质量轨迹数据对支持有效智能体训练的需求。然而，现有的轨迹合成流程生成的智能体，常常无法推广到简单交互之外。我们认为这种局限性源于对语义模糊动作的忽视，这些动作的含义依赖于上下文、顺序或视觉上的模糊性。这些动作对于真实世界的鲁棒性至关重要，但在当前数据集中代表性不足且处理效果不佳，导致任务指令和执行之间存在语义不对齐。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种硬度感知轨迹合成框架HATS，旨在减轻语义模糊的影响。我们将硬度定义为与动作相关的语义模糊程度，并开发了两个互补模块：（1）硬度驱动的探索，引导数据收集向模糊但信息丰富的交互方向发展，以及（2）对齐引导的精炼，迭代地验证和修复指令-执行对齐。这两个模块以闭环方式运行：探索为精炼提供具有挑战性的轨迹，而精炼反馈则更新硬度信号以指导未来的探索。大量实验表明，使用HATS训练的智能体在基准GUI环境中始终优于最先进的基线模型。

TLDR: The paper introduces HATS, a framework for generating high-quality GUI agent training data by addressing semantic ambiguity in actions through hardness-driven exploration and alignment-guided refinement, leading to improved agent performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了HATS，一个用于生成高质量GUI代理训练数据的框架。它通过硬度驱动探索和对齐引导改进来解决动作中的语义模糊性，从而提高代理的性能。

Authors: Rui Shao, Ruize Gao, Bin Xie, Yixing Li, Kaiwen Zhou, Shuai Wang, Weili Guan, Gongwei Chen

$Ψ_0$: An Open Foundation Model Towards Universal Humanoid Loco-Manipulation

Abstract (English): We introduce $Ψ_0$ (Psi-Zero), an open foundation model to address challenging humanoid loco-manipulation tasks. While existing approaches often attempt to address this fundamental problem by co-training on large and diverse human and humanoid data, we argue that this strategy is suboptimal due to the fundamental kinematic and motion disparities between humans and humanoid robots. Therefore, data efficiency and model performance remain unsatisfactory despite the considerable data volume. To address this challenge, \ours\;decouples the learning process to maximize the utility of heterogeneous data sources. Specifically, we propose a staged training paradigm with different learning objectives: First, we autoregressively pre-train a VLM backbone on large-scale egocentric human videos to acquire generalizable visual-action representations. Then, we post-train a flow-based action expert on high-quality humanoid robot data to learn precise robot joint control. Our research further identifies a critical yet often overlooked data recipe: in contrast to approaches that scale with noisy Internet clips or heterogeneous cross-embodiment robot datasets, we demonstrate that pre-training on high-quality egocentric human manipulation data followed by post-training on domain-specific real-world humanoid trajectories yields superior performance. Extensive real-world experiments demonstrate that \ours\ achieves the best performance using only about 800 hours of human video data and 30 hours of real-world robot data, outperforming baselines pre-trained on more than 10$\times$ as much data by over 40\% in overall success rate across multiple tasks. We will open-source the entire ecosystem to the community, including a data processing and training pipeline, a humanoid foundation model, and a real-time action inference engine.

摘要（中文）: 我们推出了$Ψ_0$（Psi-Zero），一个开放的基础模型，旨在解决具有挑战性的人形机器人抓取操作任务。虽然现有的方法通常尝试通过在大型且多样化的人类和人形机器人数据上进行联合训练来解决这个根本性问题，但我们认为这种策略并非最优，因为人类和人形机器人之间存在根本性的运动学和运动差异。因此，尽管数据量庞大，但数据效率和模型性能仍不能令人满意。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出的方法解耦了学习过程，以最大限度地提高异构数据源的利用率。具体而言，我们提出了一种具有不同学习目标的阶段式训练范式：首先，我们在大规模的第一人称视角人类视频上进行自回归的VLM骨干预训练，以获得通用的视觉-动作表征。然后，我们在高质量的人形机器人数据上后期训练一个基于流的动作专家，以学习精确的机器人关节控制。我们的研究进一步确定了一个关键但经常被忽视的数据配方：与使用嘈杂的互联网片段或异构的跨形态机器人数据集进行缩放的方法相反，我们证明，在高质量的第一人称视角人类操作数据上进行预训练，然后在特定领域的真实人形机器人轨迹上进行后期训练，可以产生卓越的性能。大量的真实世界实验表明，\ours\;仅使用约800小时的人类视频数据和30小时的真实机器人数据，就能达到最佳性能，在多个任务上的总体成功率比在多达10倍数据上预训练的基线高出40\%以上。我们将向社区开源整个生态系统，包括数据处理和训练流程、人形机器人基础模型以及实时动作推理引擎。

TLDR: The paper introduces $Ψ_0$, an open foundation model for humanoid loco-manipulation that uses a staged training paradigm: pre-training a VLM on human videos and then post-training a flow-based action expert on robot data, achieving better performance with less data compared to other approaches.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了$Ψ_0$，一个用于人形机器人移动操作的开放基础模型，它采用了一种分阶段训练范例：首先在人类视频上预训练一个VLM，然后在机器人数据上后训练一个基于流动的动作专家，与其它方法相比，它以更少的数据实现了更好的效果。

Authors: Songlin Wei, Hongyi Jing, Boqian Li, Zhenyu Zhao, Jiageng Mao, Zhenhao Ni, Sicheng He, Jie Liu, Xiawei Liu, Kaidi Kang, Sheng Zang, Weiduo Yuan, Marco Pavone, Di Huang, Yue Wang

HandelBot: Real-World Piano Playing via Fast Adaptation of Dexterous Robot Policies

Abstract (English): Mastering dexterous manipulation with multi-fingered hands has been a grand challenge in robotics for decades. Despite its potential, the difficulty of collecting high-quality data remains a primary bottleneck for high-precision tasks. While reinforcement learning and simulation-to-real-world transfer offer a promising alternative, the transferred policies often fail for tasks demanding millimeter-scale precision, such as bimanual piano playing. In this work, we introduce HandelBot, a framework that combines a simulation policy and rapid adaptation through a two-stage pipeline. Starting from a simulation-trained policy, we first apply a structured refinement stage to correct spatial alignments by adjusting lateral finger joints based on physical rollouts. Next, we use residual reinforcement learning to autonomously learn fine-grained corrective actions. Through extensive hardware experiments across five recognized songs, we demonstrate that HandelBot can successfully perform precise bimanual piano playing. Our system outperforms direct simulation deployment by a factor of 1.8x and requires only 30 minutes of physical interaction data.

摘要（中文）: 几十年来，利用多指灵巧手掌握精细操作一直是机器人领域的一项巨大挑战。尽管具有潜力，但收集高质量数据的困难仍然是实现高精度任务的主要瓶颈。强化学习和从仿真到现实世界的迁移提供了一种有希望的替代方案，但对于需要毫米级精度的任务（例如双手钢琴演奏），迁移策略通常会失效。在这项工作中，我们介绍了一个框架 HandelBot，它结合了仿真策略，并通过两阶段流水线进行快速适应。首先，从仿真训练的策略开始，我们应用结构化精炼阶段，通过基于物理展开调整横向手指关节来校正空间对齐。接下来，我们使用残差强化学习自主学习细粒度的纠正动作。通过对五首公认歌曲进行的大量硬件实验，我们证明了 HandelBot 可以成功执行精确的双手钢琴演奏。我们的系统性能比直接仿真部署提高了 1.8 倍，并且只需要 30 分钟的物理交互数据。

TLDR: HandelBot achieves precise bimanual piano playing through a two-stage pipeline of simulation-trained policy refinement and residual reinforcement learning, significantly outperforming direct simulation deployment with minimal physical interaction data.

简要说明: HandelBot通过一个两阶段流程实现了精确的双手钢琴演奏：首先是仿真训练策略的细化，然后是残差强化学习。这种方法显著优于直接仿真部署，并且只需要最少的物理交互数据。

Authors: Amber Xie, Haozhi Qi, Dorsa Sadigh

ComFree-Sim: A GPU-Parallelized Analytical Contact Physics Engine for Scalable Contact-Rich Robotics Simulation and Control

Abstract (English): Physics simulation for contact-rich robotics is often bottlenecked by contact resolution: mainstream engines enforce non-penetration and Coulomb friction via complementarity constraints or constrained optimization, requiring per-step iterative solves whose cost grows superlinearly with contact density. We present ComFree-Sim, a GPU-parallelized analytical contact physics engine built on complementarity-free contact modeling. ComFree-Sim computes contact impulses in closed form via an impedance-style prediction--correction update in the dual cone of Coulomb friction. Contact computation decouples across contact pairs and becomes separable across cone facets, mapping naturally to GPU kernels and yielding near-linear runtime scaling with the number of contacts. We further extend the formulation to a unified 6D contact model capturing tangential, torsional, and rolling friction, and introduce a practical dual-cone impedance heuristic. ComFree-Sim is implemented in Warp and exposed through a MuJoCo-compatible interface as a drop-in backend alternative to MuJoCo Warp (MJWarp). Experiments benchmark penetration, friction behaviors, stability, and simulation runtime scaling against MJWarp, demonstrating near-linear scaling and 2--3 times higher throughput in dense contact scenes with comparable physical fidelity. We deploy ComFree-Sim in real-time MPC for in-hand dexterous manipulation on a real-world multi-fingered LEAP hand and in dynamics-aware motion retargeting, demonstrating that low-latency simulation yields higher closed-loop success rates and enables practical high-frequency control in contact-rich tasks.

摘要（中文）: 在接触丰富的机器人学中，物理仿真通常受限于接触解析：主流引擎通过互补约束或约束优化来强制执行非穿透和库仑摩擦，这需要每一步进行迭代求解，其成本随接触密度的增加呈超线性增长。我们提出了ComFree-Sim，一种基于GPU并行化的解析接触物理引擎，它建立在无互补约束的接触建模之上。ComFree-Sim通过在库仑摩擦的对偶锥中使用阻抗风格的预测-校正更新，以闭合形式计算接触冲量。接触计算在接触对之间解耦，并在锥面之间分离，自然地映射到GPU内核，并产生与接触次数近乎线性的运行时伸缩性。我们进一步将该公式扩展到统一的六自由度接触模型，该模型捕捉切向、扭转和滚动摩擦，并引入一种实用的对偶锥阻抗启发式方法。ComFree-Sim在Warp中实现，并通过与MuJoCo兼容的接口作为MuJoCo Warp (MJWarp)的直接替代后端公开。实验针对MJWarp对穿透、摩擦行为、稳定性和仿真运行时伸缩性进行了基准测试，表明在具有可比物理逼真度的密集接触场景中，具有近乎线性的伸缩性和2-3倍更高的吞吐量。我们在真实多指LEAP手上的手内灵巧操作的实时MPC以及动态感知运动重定向中部署了ComFree-Sim，表明低延迟仿真能够获得更高的闭环成功率，并在接触丰富的任务中实现实用的高频控制。

TLDR: The paper introduces ComFree-Sim, a GPU-parallelized physics engine using a complementarity-free contact model for faster and more scalable contact-rich robotics simulation and control, demonstrating improved performance over MuJoCo Warp in dense contact scenarios and enabling real-time MPC for dexterous manipulation.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了ComFree-Sim，一个使用互补性无关的接触模型的GPU并行物理引擎，用于更快和更具可扩展性的富接触机器人仿真和控制。该引擎在密集接触场景中表现出比MuJoCo Warp更好的性能，并支持用于灵巧操作的实时MPC。

Authors: Chetan Borse, Zhixian Xie, Wei-Cheng Huang, Wanxin Jin

O3N: Omnidirectional Open-Vocabulary Occupancy Prediction

Abstract (English): Understanding and reconstructing the 3D world through omnidirectional perception is an inevitable trend in the development of autonomous agents and embodied intelligence. However, existing 3D occupancy prediction methods are constrained by limited perspective inputs and predefined training distribution, making them difficult to apply to embodied agents that require comprehensive and safe perception of scenes in open world exploration. To address this, we present O3N, the first purely visual, end-to-end Omnidirectional Open-vocabulary Occupancy predictioN framework. O3N embeds omnidirectional voxels in a polar-spiral topology via the Polar-spiral Mamba (PsM) module, enabling continuous spatial representation and long-range context modeling across 360°. The Occupancy Cost Aggregation (OCA) module introduces a principled mechanism for unifying geometric and semantic supervision within the voxel space, ensuring consistency between the reconstructed geometry and the underlying semantic structure. Moreover, Natural Modality Alignment (NMA) establishes a gradient-free alignment pathway that harmonizes visual features, voxel embeddings, and text semantics, forming a consistent "pixel-voxel-text" representation triad. Extensive experiments on multiple models demonstrate that our method not only achieves state-of-the-art performance on QuadOcc and Human360Occ benchmarks but also exhibits remarkable cross-scene generalization and semantic scalability, paving the way toward universal 3D world modeling. The source code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/MengfeiD/O3N.

摘要（中文）: 通过全向感知理解和重建3D世界是自主代理和具身智能发展不可避免的趋势。然而，现有的3D占据预测方法受到有限视角输入和预定义训练分布的限制，使其难以应用于需要全面和安全地感知开放世界场景的具身代理。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了O3N，这是第一个纯视觉、端到端的全向开放词汇占据预测框架。O3N通过极坐标-螺旋Mamba（PsM）模块将全向体素嵌入到极坐标-螺旋拓扑中，从而实现连续的空间表示和360°范围内的长程上下文建模。占据代价聚合（OCA）模块引入了一种原则性的机制，用于统一体素空间内的几何和语义监督，确保重建的几何体与底层语义结构之间的一致性。此外，自然模态对齐（NMA）建立了一条无梯度对齐通路，协调视觉特征、体素嵌入和文本语义，形成一个一致的“像素-体素-文本”表示三元组。在多个模型上进行的大量实验表明，我们的方法不仅在QuadOcc和Human360Occ基准测试上取得了最先进的性能，而且表现出卓越的跨场景泛化能力和语义可扩展性，为通用3D世界建模铺平了道路。源代码将在https://github.com/MengfeiD/O3N公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces O3N, a novel framework for omnidirectional open-vocabulary occupancy prediction using a polar-spiral voxel embedding, occupancy cost aggregation, and natural modality alignment for consistent pixel-voxel-text representation, achieving SOTA results with strong generalization.

简要说明: 该论文提出了O3N，一种新颖的用于全方位开放词汇占用预测的框架，它使用极坐标螺旋体素嵌入、占用成本聚合和自然模态对齐，以实现一致的像素-体素-文本表示，并取得了最先进的结果和强大的泛化能力。

Authors: Mengfei Duan, Hao Shi, Fei Teng, Guoqiang Zhao, Yuheng Zhang, Zhiyong Li, Kailun Yang

Learning Visuomotor Policy for Multi-Robot Laser Tag Game

Abstract (English): In this paper, we study multi robot laser tag, a simplified yet practical shooting-game-style task. Classic modular approaches on these tasks face challenges such as limited observability and reliance on depth mapping and inter robot communication. To overcome these issues, we present an end-to-end visuomotor policy that maps images directly to robot actions. We train a high performing teacher policy with multi agent reinforcement learning and distill its knowledge into a vision-based student policy. Technical designs, including a permutation-invariant feature extractor and depth heatmap input, improve performance over standard architectures. Our policy outperforms classic methods by 16.7% in hitting accuracy and 6% in collision avoidance, and is successfully deployed on real robots. Code will be released publicly.

摘要（中文）: 本文研究多机器人激光枪战，这是一个简化但实用的射击游戏风格任务。针对这类任务的经典模块化方法面临着一些挑战，如有限的可观测性以及对深度映射和机器人间通信的依赖。为了克服这些问题，我们提出了一种端到端视觉运动策略，该策略将图像直接映射到机器人动作。我们利用多智能体强化学习训练了一个高性能的教师策略，并将其知识提炼到一个基于视觉的学生策略中。包括置换不变特征提取器和深度热图输入在内的技术设计，改进了超出标准架构的性能。我们的策略在命中精度方面优于经典方法16.7%，在避障方面优于6%，并且已成功部署在真实机器人上。代码将公开发布。

TLDR: This paper presents an end-to-end visuomotor policy for multi-robot laser tag, trained with reinforcement learning and distillation, achieving improved performance and real-world deployment.

Authors: Kai Li, Shiyu Zhao

SVLL: Staged Vision-Language Learning for Physically Grounded Embodied Task Planning

Abstract (English): Embodied task planning demands vision-language models to generate action sequences that are both visually grounded and causally coherent over time. However, existing training paradigms face a critical trade-off: joint end-to-end training often leads to premature temporal binding, while standard reinforcement learning methods suffer from optimization instability. To bridge this gap, we present Staged Vision-Language Learning (SVLL), a unified three-stage framework for robust, physically-grounded embodied planning. In the first two stages, SVLL decouples spatial grounding from temporal reasoning, establishing robust visual dependency before introducing sequential action history. In the final stage, we identify a key limitation of standard Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), its purely relative nature -- optimizing only the preference gap between winning and losing trajectories while neglecting absolute likelihood constraints on optimal path, often yields unsafe or hallucinated behaviors. To address this, we further introduce Bias-DPO, a novel alignment objective that injects an inductive bias toward expert trajectories by explicitly maximizing likelihood on ground-truth actions while penalizing overconfident hallucinations. By anchoring the policy to the expert manifold and mitigating causal misalignment, SVLL, powered by Bias-DPO, ensures strict adherence to environmental affordances and effectively suppresses physically impossible shortcuts. Finally, extensive experiments on the interactive AI2-THOR benchmark and real-world robotic deployments demonstrate that SVLL outperforms both state-of-the-art open-source (e.g., Qwen2.5-VL-7B) and closed-source models (e.g., GPT-4o, Gemini-2.0-flash) in task success rate, while significantly reducing physical constraint violations.

摘要（中文）: 具身任务规划要求视觉-语言模型生成在视觉上具有基础且在时间上因果连贯的动作序列。然而，现有的训练范式面临着一个关键的权衡：联合端到端训练通常导致过早的时间绑定，而标准强化学习方法则受到优化不稳定性的困扰。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了分阶段视觉-语言学习 (SVLL)，这是一个统一的三阶段框架，用于实现鲁棒的、物理基础的具身规划。在前两个阶段，SVLL将空间基础与时间推理分离，在引入顺序动作历史之前，建立稳健的视觉依赖关系。在最后阶段，我们识别了标准直接偏好优化 (DPO) 的一个关键限制，即其纯粹的相对性——仅优化获胜和失败轨迹之间的偏好差距，而忽略了对最优路径的绝对似然约束，这通常会导致不安全或虚假的动作。为了解决这个问题，我们进一步引入了 Bias-DPO，这是一种新颖的对齐目标，通过显式地最大化真实动作的似然性，同时惩罚过度自信的幻觉，将一种对专家轨迹的归纳偏置注入其中。通过将策略锚定到专家流形并减轻因果错位，由 Bias-DPO 驱动的 SVLL 确保严格遵守环境可供性，并有效抑制物理上不可能的捷径。最后，在交互式 AI2-THOR 基准测试和真实机器人部署上的大量实验表明，SVLL 在任务成功率方面优于最先进的开源模型（例如，Qwen2.5-VL-7B）和闭源模型（例如，GPT-4o、Gemini-2.0-flash），同时显著减少了物理约束违规。

TLDR: This paper introduces SVLL, a three-stage vision-language learning framework with a novel Bias-DPO objective, for physically grounded embodied task planning, demonstrating improvements over SOTA models on AI2-THOR and real robots.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为SVLL的三阶段视觉语言学习框架，它具有一种新颖的Bias-DPO目标，用于物理接地的具身任务规划，并在AI2-THOR和真实机器人上展示了优于SOTA模型的改进。

Authors: Yuyuan Yang, Junkun Hong, Hongrong Wang, Honghao Cai, Xunpeng Ren, Ge Wang, Mingcong Lei, Shenhao Yan, Jiahao Yang, Chengsi Yao, Xi Li, Yiming Zhao, Yatong Han, Jinke Ren

RoboClaw: An Agentic Framework for Scalable Long-Horizon Robotic Tasks

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) systems have shown strong potential for language-driven robotic manipulation. However, scaling them to long-horizon tasks remains challenging. Existing pipelines typically separate data collection, policy learning, and deployment, resulting in heavy reliance on manual environment resets and brittle multi-policy execution. We present RoboClaw, an agentic robotics framework that unifies data collection, policy learning, and task execution under a single VLM-driven controller. At the policy level, RoboClaw introduces Entangled Action Pairs (EAP), which couple forward manipulation behaviors with inverse recovery actions to form self-resetting loops for autonomous data collection. This mechanism enables continuous on-policy data acquisition and iterative policy refinement with minimal human intervention. During deployment, the same agent performs high-level reasoning and dynamically orchestrates learned policy primitives to accomplish long-horizon tasks. By maintaining consistent contextual semantics across collection and execution, RoboClaw reduces mismatch between the two phases and improves multi-policy robustness. Experiments in real-world manipulation tasks demonstrate improved stability and scalability compared to conventional open-loop pipelines, while significantly reducing human effort throughout the robot lifecycle, achieving a 25% improvement in success rate over baseline methods on long-horizon tasks and reducing human time investment by 53.7%.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 系统在语言驱动的机器人操作方面展现出强大的潜力。然而，将其扩展到长时程任务仍然具有挑战性。现有的流程通常将数据采集、策略学习和部署分开，导致严重依赖手动环境重置和脆弱的多策略执行。我们提出了 RoboClaw，一个智能体机器人框架，它在单个 VLM 驱动的控制器下统一了数据采集、策略学习和任务执行。在策略层面，RoboClaw 引入了纠缠动作对 (EAP)，它将正向操作行为与反向恢复动作相耦合，形成用于自主数据采集的自重置循环。这种机制实现了持续的在线策略数据获取以及以最小的人工干预进行迭代的策略优化。在部署期间，同一个智能体执行高级推理，并动态地编排学习到的策略基元以完成长时程任务。通过在采集和执行过程中保持一致的上下文语义，RoboClaw 减少了这两个阶段之间的不匹配，并提高了多策略的鲁棒性。在真实世界操作任务中的实验表明，与传统的开环流程相比，RoboClaw 提高了稳定性和可扩展性，同时显著减少了机器人的整个生命周期内的人力投入，在长时程任务上的成功率比基线方法提高了 25%，并减少了 53.7% 的人工时间投入。

TLDR: RoboClaw is an agentic robotics framework that unifies data collection, policy learning, and task execution using a VLM-driven controller with self-resetting loops for improved scalability and reduced human intervention in long-horizon robotic tasks. The key idea revolves around 'Entangled Action Pairs' for continuous on-policy data acquisition.

简要说明: RoboClaw 是一种代理机器人框架，它统一了数据收集、策略学习和任务执行，使用 VLM 驱动的控制器和自重置循环，以提高长期机器人任务的可扩展性并减少人为干预。其关键思想围绕“纠缠行动对”进行，以实现持续的在线策略数据采集。

Authors: Ruiying Li, Yunlang Zhou, YuYao Zhu, Kylin Chen, Jingyuan Wang, Sukai Wang, Kongtao Hu, Minhui Yu, Bowen Jiang, Zhan Su, Jiayao Ma, Xin He, Yongjian Shen, Yangyang, Guanghui Ren, Maoqing Yao, Wenhao Wang, Yao Mu

CoViLLM: An Adaptive Human-Robot Collaborative Assembly Framework Using Large Language Models for Manufacturing

Abstract (English): With increasing demand for mass customization, traditional manufacturing robots that rely on rule-based operations lack the flexibility to accommodate customized or new product variants. Human-Robot Collaboration (HRC) has demonstrated potential to improve system adaptability by leveraging human versatility and decision-making capabilities. However, existing HRC frame- works typically depend on predefined perception-manipulation pipelines, limiting their ability to autonomously generate task plans for new product assembly. In this work, we propose CoViLLM, an adaptive human-robot collaborative assembly frame- work that supports the assembly of customized and previously unseen products. CoViLLM combines depth-camera-based localization for object position estimation, human operator classification for identifying new components, and an Large Language Model (LLM) for assembly task planning based on natural language instructions. The framework is validated on the NIST Assembly Task Board for known, customized, and new product cases. Experimental results show that the proposed framework enables flexible collaborative assembly by extending HRC beyond predefined product and task settings.

摘要（中文）: 随着对大规模定制需求的日益增长，依赖于基于规则操作的传统制造机器人缺乏适应定制或新产品变体的灵活性。人机协作(HRC)通过利用人类的多功能性和决策能力，展现出提高系统适应性的潜力。然而，现有的人机协作框架通常依赖于预定义的感知-操作流水线，限制了其自主生成新产品装配任务计划的能力。在这项工作中，我们提出CoViLLM，一种自适应的人机协作装配框架，支持定制和以前未见过的产品的装配。CoViLLM结合了基于深度相机的定位以进行物体位置估计，用于识别新组件的人工操作员分类，以及用于基于自然语言指令进行装配任务规划的大型语言模型(LLM)。该框架在NIST装配任务板上针对已知、定制和新产品案例进行了验证。实验结果表明，所提出的框架通过将人机协作扩展到预定义的产品和任务设置之外，实现了灵活的协作装配。

TLDR: This paper introduces CoViLLM, an LLM-based framework for adaptive human-robot collaborative assembly that can handle customized and new products by integrating depth-camera localization, human operator classification, and LLM-based task planning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CoViLLM，一个基于大型语言模型的自适应人机协作装配框架，通过整合基于深度相机的定位，人工操作员识别和基于大型语言模型的任务规划，能够处理定制化和全新的产品。

Authors: Jiabao Zhao, Jonghan Lim, Hongliang Li, Ilya Kovalenko

Grounding Robot Generalization in Training Data via Retrieval-Augmented VLMs

Abstract (English): Recent work on robot manipulation has advanced policy generalization to novel scenarios. However, it is often difficult to characterize how different evaluation settings actually represent generalization from the training distribution of a given policy. To work towards more precise evaluation of generalization in robotics, we propose RADAR, a scalable framework for directly comparing test-time evaluation tasks to policy training data, to determine what form of policy generalization is required. RADAR consists of a two-stage pipeline: first, retrieval using generalist policy embeddings identifies which training examples are relevant for a given evaluation task. Next, vision-language models (VLMs) analyze the evaluation task against the retrieved data, outputting interpretable analysis on how they compare along a variety of axes, and an overall classification of what type of policy generalization is required. Through controlled experiments, we demonstrate that VLMs are effective at analyzing data for generalization, and that our retrieval step effectively identifies examples needed to make accurate classifications with respect to the training data. Furthermore, we scale RADAR to large-scale datasets, where we observe agreement with human-defined benchmark conditions from prior work. We provide demonstrations at radar-analysis.github.io.

摘要（中文）: 机器人操作领域的最新研究已推进策略泛化到新的场景。然而，通常难以描述不同的评估设置如何真实地代表给定策略从训练分布的泛化能力。为了更精确地评估机器人领域的泛化能力，我们提出了 RADAR，一个可扩展的框架，能够直接比较测试时的评估任务与策略训练数据，以确定所需的策略泛化形式。RADAR 由一个两阶段流程组成：首先，利用通用策略嵌入进行检索，识别与给定评估任务相关的训练示例。然后，视觉-语言模型 (VLMs) 分析评估任务与检索到的数据，输出可解释的分析结果，说明它们在多个维度上的比较情况，并对所需的策略泛化类型进行总体分类。通过受控实验，我们证明了 VLMs 在泛化数据分析方面的有效性，并且我们的检索步骤能够有效识别做出关于训练数据的准确分类所需的示例。此外，我们将 RADAR 扩展到大规模数据集，观察到其结果与先前工作中人类定义的基准条件相符。我们将在 radar-analysis.github.io 上提供演示。

TLDR: The paper introduces RADAR, a framework using policy embeddings and vision-language models to analyze the type of generalization required for robot manipulation tasks by comparing them to training data.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RADAR，一个使用策略嵌入和视觉语言模型来分析机器人操作任务所需的泛化类型的框架，通过将它们与训练数据进行比较。

Authors: Jensen Gao, Dorsa Sadigh, Sandy Huang, Dhruv Shah

Deployment-Time Reliability of Learned Robot Policies

Abstract (English): Recent advances in learning-based robot manipulation have produced policies with remarkable capabilities. Yet, reliability at deployment remains a fundamental barrier to real-world use, where distribution shift, compounding errors, and complex task dependencies collectively undermine system performance. This dissertation investigates how the reliability of learned robot policies can be improved at deployment time through mechanisms that operate around them. We develop three complementary classes of deployment-time mechanisms. First, we introduce runtime monitoring methods that detect impending failures by identifying inconsistencies in closed-loop policy behavior and deviations in task progress, without requiring failure data or task-specific supervision. Second, we propose a data-centric framework for policy interpretability that traces deployment-time successes and failures to influential training demonstrations using influence functions, enabling principled diagnosis and dataset curation. Third, we address reliable long-horizon task execution by formulating policy coordination as the problem of estimating and maximizing the success probability of behavior sequences, and we extend this formulation to open-ended, language-specified tasks through feasibility-aware task planning. By centering on core challenges of deployment, these contributions advance practical foundations for the reliable, real-world use of learned robot policies. Continued progress on these foundations will be essential for enabling trustworthy and scalable robot autonomy in the future.

摘要（中文）: 基于学习的机器人操作领域的最新进展产生了具有卓越能力的策略。然而，部署时的可靠性仍然是实际应用的基本障碍，其中分布偏移、累积误差和复杂的任务依赖性共同削弱系统性能。 该论文研究了如何在部署时通过围绕学习到的机器人策略运行的机制来提高其可靠性。我们开发了三类互补的部署时机制。 首先，我们引入了运行时监控方法，通过识别闭环策略行为中的不一致性和任务进展中的偏差来检测即将发生的故障，而无需故障数据或特定于任务的监督。 其次，我们提出了一个以数据为中心的策略可解释性框架，使用影响函数将部署时的成功和失败追溯到有影响力的训练演示，从而实现有原则的诊断和数据集整理。 第三，我们通过将策略协调公式化为估计和最大化行为序列成功概率的问题，来解决可靠的长周期任务执行问题，并通过可行性感知的任务规划将此公式扩展到开放式、语言指定的任务。 通过专注于部署的核心挑战，这些贡献为学习到的机器人策略的可靠的、实际应用奠定了基础。 在这些基础上的持续进展对于未来实现可信赖且可扩展的机器人自主至关重要。

TLDR: This dissertation focuses on improving the deployment-time reliability of learned robot policies through runtime monitoring, data-centric policy interpretability using influence functions, and policy coordination for long-horizon tasks, addressing critical challenges for real-world robot autonomy.

简要说明: 该论文重点研究如何通过运行时监控、基于影响函数的数据中心策略可解释性以及用于长时程任务的策略协调来提高学习型机器人策略在部署时的可靠性，从而解决实际机器人自主性的关键挑战。

Authors: Christopher Agia

Novelty Adaptation Through Hybrid Large Language Model (LLM)-Symbolic Planning and LLM-guided Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): In dynamic open-world environments, autonomous agents often encounter novelties that hinder their ability to find plans to achieve their goals. Specifically, traditional symbolic planners fail to generate plans when the robot's planning domain lacks the operators that enable it to interact appropriately with novel objects in the environment. We propose a neuro-symbolic architecture that integrates symbolic planning, reinforcement learning, and a large language model (LLM) to learn how to handle novel objects. In particular, we leverage the common sense reasoning capability of the LLM to identify missing operators, generate plans with the symbolic AI planner, and write reward functions to guide the reinforcement learning agent in learning control policies for newly identified operators. Our method outperforms the state-of-the-art methods in operator discovery as well as operator learning in continuous robotic domains.

摘要（中文）: 在动态开放世界环境中，自主体经常遇到阻碍其实现目标的创新性事物。具体而言，当机器人的规划域缺少使其能够与环境中新颖物体适当交互的算子时，传统的符号规划器便无法生成计划。我们提出了一种神经符号架构，该架构集成了符号规划、强化学习和大型语言模型 (LLM)，以学习如何处理新颖物体。特别地，我们利用 LLM 的常识推理能力来识别缺失的算子，使用符号 AI 规划器生成计划，并编写奖励函数来指导强化学习体学习针对新识别算子的控制策略。我们的方法在算子发现以及连续机器人域中的算子学习方面均优于最先进的方法。

TLDR: This paper introduces a neuro-symbolic architecture that uses LLMs to discover missing operators in symbolic planning, generate plans, and create reward functions for RL to learn control policies for novel objects in dynamic environments, demonstrating improved performance in operator discovery and learning.

Authors: Hong Lu, Pierrick Lorang, Timothy R. Duggan, Jivko Sinapov, Matthias Scheutz

Learning to Assist: Physics-Grounded Human-Human Control via Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Humanoid robotics has strong potential to transform daily service and caregiving applications. Although recent advances in general motion tracking within physics engines (GMT) have enabled virtual characters and humanoid robots to reproduce a broad range of human motions, these behaviors are primarily limited to contact-less social interactions or isolated movements. Assistive scenarios, by contrast, require continuous awareness of a human partner and rapid adaptation to their evolving posture and dynamics. In this paper, we formulate the imitation of closely interacting, force-exchanging human-human motion sequences as a multi-agent reinforcement learning problem. We jointly train partner-aware policies for both the supporter (assistant) agent and the recipient agent in a physics simulator to track assistive motion references. To make this problem tractable, we introduce a partner policies initialization scheme that transfers priors from single-human motion-tracking controllers, greatly improving exploration. We further propose dynamic reference retargeting and contact-promoting reward, which adapt the assistant's reference motion to the recipient's real-time pose and encourage physically meaningful support. We show that AssistMimic is the first method capable of successfully tracking assistive interaction motions on established benchmarks, demonstrating the benefits of a multi-agent RL formulation for physically grounded and socially aware humanoid control.

摘要（中文）: 人形机器人具有改变日常服务和照护应用的巨大潜力。尽管物理引擎中的通用运动追踪（GMT）的最新进展已使虚拟角色和人形机器人能够再现广泛的人类运动，但这些行为主要局限于无接触的社交互动或孤立的动作。相比之下，辅助场景需要持续感知人类伙伴并快速适应他们不断变化的姿势和动态。在本文中，我们将密切互动的，力交换的人与人运动序列的模仿建模为一个多智能体强化学习问题。我们在物理模拟器中联合训练支持者（助手）智能体和接受者智能体的伙伴感知策略，以追踪辅助运动参考。为了使这个问题易于处理，我们引入了一种伙伴策略初始化方案，该方案可从单人运动追踪控制器迁移先验知识，从而大大改善探索。我们进一步提出了动态参考重定向和接触促进奖励，以使助手的参考运动适应接受者的实时姿态，并鼓励具有物理意义的支持。我们证明AssistMimic是第一个能够在已建立的基准测试中成功跟踪辅助互动运动的方法，证明了多智能体强化学习公式在物理基础和社交感知人形机器人控制方面的优势。

TLDR: This paper proposes a multi-agent reinforcement learning approach for humanoid robots to assist humans in force-exchanging tasks, using novel initialization and reward shaping techniques to achieve successful assistive motion tracking. It pioneers the ability to track assistive human-human interaction motions on established benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种多智能体强化学习方法，用于人形机器人协助人类完成力交换任务，利用新颖的初始化和奖励塑造技术，实现了成功的辅助运动跟踪。该方法率先能够跟踪现有基准上的辅助人与人互动运动。

Authors: Yuto Shibata, Kashu Yamazaki, Lalit Jayanti, Yoshimitsu Aoki, Mariko Isogawa, Katerina Fragkiadaki

BehaviorVLM: Unified Finetuning-Free Behavioral Understanding with Vision-Language Reasoning

Abstract (English): Understanding freely moving animal behavior is central to neuroscience, where pose estimation and behavioral understanding form the foundation for linking neural activity to natural actions. Yet both tasks still depend heavily on human annotation or unstable unsupervised pipelines, limiting scalability and reproducibility. We present BehaviorVLM, a unified vision-language framework for pose estimation and behavioral understanding that requires no task-specific finetuning and minimal human labeling by guiding pretrained Vision-Language Models (VLMs) through detailed, explicit, and verifiable reasoning steps. For pose estimation, we leverage quantum-dot-grounded behavioral data and propose a multi-stage pipeline that integrates temporal, spatial, and cross-view reasoning. This design greatly reduces human annotation effort, exposes low-confidence labels through geometric checks such as reprojection error, and produces labels that can later be filtered, corrected, or used to fine-tune downstream pose models. For behavioral understanding, we propose a pipeline that integrates deep embedded clustering for over-segmented behavior discovery, VLM-based per-clip video captioning, and LLM-based reasoning to merge and semantically label behavioral segments. The behavioral pipeline can operate directly from visual information and does not require keypoints to segment behavior. Together, these components enable scalable, interpretable, and label-light analysis of multi-animal behavior.

摘要（中文）: 理解自由移动动物的行为是神经科学的核心，其中姿态估计和行为理解构成了将神经活动与自然行为联系起来的基础。然而，这两项任务仍然严重依赖于人工标注或不稳定的无监督流程，限制了可扩展性和可重复性。我们提出了 BehaviorVLM，一个统一的视觉-语言框架，用于姿态估计和行为理解，它不需要任何特定于任务的微调，并通过详细、明确和可验证的推理步骤指导预训练的视觉-语言模型（VLMs），从而最大程度地减少人工标记。对于姿态估计，我们利用量子点接地的行为数据，并提出了一个集成时间、空间和跨视角推理的多阶段流程。这种设计极大地减少了人工标注工作量，通过诸如重投影误差等几何检查暴露了低置信度标签，并生成了随后可以过滤、校正或用于微调下游姿态模型的标签。对于行为理解，我们提出了一个流程，该流程集成了用于过度分割行为发现的深度嵌入聚类、基于VLM的逐clip视频字幕和基于LLM的推理，以合并和语义化标注行为片段。行为流水线可以直接从视觉信息操作，不需要关键点来分割行为。总而言之，这些组件实现了对多动物行为的可扩展、可解释和轻量级标签分析。

TLDR: BehaviorVLM is a finetuning-free vision-language framework for animal pose estimation and behavior understanding, requiring minimal human labeling by leveraging pretrained VLMs and LLMs with explicit reasoning steps.

Authors: Jingyang Ke, Weihan Li, Amartya Pradhan, Jeffrey Markowitz, Anqi Wu

IsoCompute Playbook: Optimally Scaling Sampling Compute for LLM RL

Abstract (English): While scaling laws guide compute allocation for LLM pre-training, analogous prescriptions for reinforcement learning (RL) post-training of large language models (LLMs) remain poorly understood. We study the compute-optimal allocation of sampling compute for on-policy RL methods in LLMs, framing scaling as a compute-constrained optimization over three resources: parallel rollouts per problem, number of problems per batch, and number of update steps. We find that the compute-optimal number of parallel rollouts per problem increases predictably with compute budget and then saturates. This trend holds across both easy and hard problems, though driven by different mechanisms: solution sharpening on easy problems and coverage expansion on hard problems. We further show that increasing the number of parallel rollouts mitigates interference across problems, while the number of problems per batch primarily affects training stability and can be chosen within a broad range. Validated across base models and data distributions, our results recast RL scaling laws as prescriptive allocation rules and provide practical guidance for compute-efficient LLM RL post-training.

摘要（中文）: 虽然缩放定律指导了 LLM 预训练的计算资源分配，但对于大型语言模型 (LLM) 的强化学习 (RL) 后训练，类似的指导原则仍然知之甚少。我们研究了 LLM 中基于策略的 RL 方法的抽样计算的最优分配，将缩放视为在计算资源约束下对三个资源进行优化的过程：每个问题的并行 rollout 数量、每个批次的问题数量和更新步数。我们发现，每个问题的计算最优并行 rollout 数量随着计算预算的增加可预测地增加，然后饱和。这种趋势在简单和困难的问题上都成立，但由不同的机制驱动：简单问题上的解决方案锐化和困难问题上的覆盖范围扩展。我们进一步表明，增加并行 rollout 的数量可以减轻问题之间的干扰，而每个批次的问题数量主要影响训练的稳定性，并且可以在一个较宽的范围内选择。我们的结果经过基础模型和数据分布的验证，将 RL 缩放定律重新定义为规定性的分配规则，并为计算高效的 LLM RL 后训练提供实用指导。

TLDR: The paper investigates compute-optimal allocation strategies for scaling on-policy RL fine-tuning of LLMs, providing practical guidance for efficient resource utilization.

简要说明: 该论文研究了针对LLM的on-policy RL微调的计算最优分配策略，为高效利用资源提供了实践指导。

Authors: Zhoujun Cheng, Yutao Xie, Yuxiao Qu, Amrith Setlur, Shibo Hao, Varad Pimpalkhute, Tongtong Liang, Feng Yao, Zhengzhong Liu, Eric Xing, Virginia Smith, Ruslan Salakhutdinov, Zhiting Hu, Taylor Killian, Aviral Kumar

Automatic Generation of High-Performance RL Environments

Abstract (English): Translating complex reinforcement learning (RL) environments into high-performance implementations has traditionally required months of specialized engineering. We present a reusable recipe - a generic prompt template, hierarchical verification, and iterative agent-assisted repair - that produces semantically equivalent high-performance environments for <$10 in compute cost. We demonstrate three distinct workflows across five environments. Direct translation (no prior performance implementation exists): EmuRust (1.5x PPO speedup via Rust parallelism for a Game Boy emulator) and PokeJAX, the first GPU-parallel Pokemon battle simulator (500M SPS random action, 15.2M SPS PPO; 22,320x over the TypeScript reference). Translation verified against existing performance implementations: throughput parity with MJX (1.04x) and 5x over Brax at matched GPU batch sizes (HalfCheetah JAX); 42x PPO (Puffer Pong). New environment creation: TCGJax, the first deployable JAX Pokemon TCG engine (717K SPS random action, 153K SPS PPO; 6.6x over the Python reference), synthesized from a web-extracted specification. At 200M parameters, the environment overhead drops below 4% of training time. Hierarchical verification (property, interaction, and rollout tests) confirms semantic equivalence for all five environments; cross-backend policy transfer confirms zero sim-to-sim gap for all five environments. TCGJax, synthesized from a private reference absent from public repositories, serves as a contamination control for agent pretraining data concerns. The paper contains sufficient detail - including representative prompts, verification methodology, and complete results - that a coding agent could reproduce the translations directly from the manuscript.

摘要（中文）: 将复杂的强化学习(RL)环境转化为高性能实现通常需要数月专业的工程工作。我们提出了一种可复用的方法——通用提示模板、分层验证和迭代的agent辅助修复——能够以低于10美元的计算成本生成语义等价的高性能环境。我们展示了跨越五个环境的三种不同的工作流程。直接翻译（不存在先前的性能实现）：EmuRust（通过Rust并行化为Game Boy模拟器带来1.5倍的PPO速度提升）和PokeJAX，首个GPU并行Pokemon战斗模拟器（5亿SPS随机动作，1520万SPS PPO；比TypeScript参考实现快22320倍）。针对现有性能实现验证的翻译：与MJX的吞吐量对等(1.04x)以及在匹配GPU批处理大小的情况下比Brax快5倍(HalfCheetah JAX)；42倍PPO（Puffer Pong）。新环境创建：TCGJax，首个可部署的JAX Pokemon TCG引擎（71.7万SPS随机动作，15.3万SPS PPO；比Python参考实现快6.6倍），从网络提取的规范合成。在2亿参数下，环境开销降至训练时间的4%以下。分层验证（属性、交互和rollout测试）确认了所有五个环境的语义等价性；跨后端策略迁移确认了所有五个环境的零sim-to-sim差距。TCGJax，从公共仓库中没有的私有参考实现合成，可作为agent预训练数据质量的污染控制。本文包含足够的细节——包括代表性提示、验证方法和完整结果——使得编码agent可以直接从手稿中重现这些翻译。

TLDR: This paper presents an automated method for generating high-performance reinforcement learning environments, demonstrating significant speedups and semantic equivalence across multiple environments using a combination of prompt engineering, hierarchical verification, and agent-assisted repair.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种自动生成高性能强化学习环境的方法，并通过提示工程、分层验证和智能体辅助修复相结合，在多个环境中实现了显著的加速和语义等价性。

Authors: Seth Karten, Rahul Dev Appapogu, Chi Jin

On Information Self-Locking in Reinforcement Learning for Active Reasoning of LLM agents

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) with outcome-based rewards has achieved significant success in training large language model (LLM) agents for complex reasoning tasks. However, in active reasoning where agents need to strategically ask questions to acquire task-relevant information, we find that LLM agents trained with RL often suffer from information self-locking: the agent ceases to ask informative questions and struggles to internalize already-obtained information. To understand the phenomenon, we decompose active reasoning into two core capabilities: Action Selection (AS), which determines the observation stream through queries, and Belief Tracking (BT), which updates the agent's belief based on collected evidence. We show that deficient AS and BT capabilities will limit the information exploration during RL training. Furthermore, insufficient exploration in turn hinders the improvement of AS and BT, creating a feedback loop that locks the agent in a low-information regime. To resolve the issue, we propose a simple yet effective approach that reallocates the learning signal by injecting easy- to-obtain directional critiques to help the agent escape self-locking. Extensive experiments with 7 datasets show that our approach significantly mitigates the information self-locking, bringing up to 60% improvements.

摘要（中文）: 基于结果的奖励强化学习（RL）在训练大型语言模型（LLM）智能体执行复杂推理任务方面取得了显著成功。然而，在主动推理中，智能体需要策略性地提问以获取任务相关信息，我们发现，使用RL训练的LLM智能体通常会遭受信息自锁：智能体停止提出有用的问题，并且难以消化已获取的信息。为了理解这种现象，我们将主动推理分解为两个核心能力：行动选择（AS），它通过查询决定观察流；以及信念追踪（BT），它基于收集到的证据更新智能体的信念。我们表明，AS和BT能力的不足会限制RL训练期间的信息探索。更进一步，探索的不足反过来又阻碍了AS和BT的改进，形成一个反馈循环，将智能体锁定在一个低信息状态。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种简单而有效的方法，通过注入易于获得的定向评论重新分配学习信号，以帮助智能体摆脱自锁。使用7个数据集的大量实验表明，我们的方法显著缓解了信息自锁，最高提升了60%。

TLDR: The paper identifies and addresses an 'information self-locking' issue in RL-trained LLM agents for active reasoning, where agents fail to ask informative questions. They propose a method to reallocate learning signals to mitigate this problem, demonstrating significant improvements across multiple datasets.

简要说明: 该论文发现并解决了RL训练的LLM智能体在主动推理中存在的“信息自锁”问题，即智能体无法提出有效的问题。他们提出了一种重新分配学习信号的方法来缓解这个问题，并在多个数据集上展示了显著的改进。

Authors: Deyu Zou, Yongqiang Chen, Fan Feng, Mufei Li, Pan Li, Yu Gong, James Cheng

XSkill: Continual Learning from Experience and Skills in Multimodal Agents

Abstract (English): Multimodal agents can now tackle complex reasoning tasks with diverse tools, yet they still suffer from inefficient tool use and inflexible orchestration in open-ended settings. A central challenge is enabling such agents to continually improve without parameter updates by learning from past trajectories. We identify two complementary forms of reusable knowledge essential for this goal: experiences, providing concise action-level guidance for tool selection and decision making, and skills, providing structured task-level guidance for planning and tool use. To this end, we propose XSkill, a dual-stream framework for continual learning from experience and skills in multimodal agents. XSkill grounds both knowledge extraction and retrieval in visual observations. During accumulation, XSkill distills and consolidates experiences and skills from multi-path rollouts via visually grounded summarization and cross-rollout critique. During inference, it retrieves and adapts this knowledge to the current visual context and feeds usage history back into accumulation to form a continual learning loop. Evaluated on five benchmarks across diverse domains with four backbone models, XSkill consistently and substantially outperforms both tool-only and learning-based baselines. Further analysis reveals that the two knowledge streams play complementary roles in influencing the reasoning behaviors of agents and show superior zero-shot generalization.

摘要（中文）: 多模态智能体现在可以利用各种工具处理复杂的推理任务，但在开放环境中，它们仍然存在工具使用效率低下和编排不灵活的问题。一个核心挑战是如何让智能体通过学习过去的轨迹来持续改进，而无需更新参数。我们认为，实现这一目标需要两种互补的可重用知识形式：经验，为工具选择和决策提供简洁的行动层面的指导；以及技能，为规划和工具使用提供结构化的任务层面指导。为此，我们提出了一种双流框架XSkill，用于多模态智能体中从经验和技能中持续学习。XSkill将知识提取和检索都与视觉观察相关联。在积累阶段，XSkill通过视觉基础的总结和跨轨迹的评估，从多路径展开中提炼和整合经验和技能。在推理阶段，它检索并将这些知识应用于当前的视觉环境，并将使用历史反馈回积累阶段，从而形成一个持续学习的循环。在五个跨领域、四个骨干模型的基准测试中，XSkill始终且显著地优于仅使用工具和基于学习的基线方法。进一步的分析表明，这两个知识流在影响智能体的推理行为方面发挥着互补作用，并表现出优越的零样本泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces XSkill, a framework that enables multimodal agents to continually learn from experience and skills, improving tool use and orchestration in open-ended settings without parameter updates. It uses visually grounded summarization and cross-rollout critique to consolidate and retrieve knowledge.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了XSkill，一个使多模态智能体能够持续从经验和技能中学习的框架，从而在开放式环境中改进工具使用和编排，无需参数更新。 它使用视觉基础汇总和交叉推广评论来巩固和检索知识。

Authors: Guanyu Jiang, Zhaochen Su, Xiaoye Qu, Yi R., Fung

Can RL Improve Generalization of LLM Agents? An Empirical Study

Abstract (English): Reinforcement fine-tuning (RFT) has shown promise for training LLM agents to perform multi-turn decision-making based on environment feedback. However, most existing evaluations remain largely in-domain: training and testing are conducted in the same environment or even on the same tasks. In real-world deployment, agents may operate in unseen environments with different background knowledge, observation spaces, and action interfaces. To characterize the generalization profile of RFT under such shifts, we conduct a systematic study along three axes: (1) within-environment generalization across task difficulty, (2) cross-environment transfer to unseen environments, and (3) sequential multi-environment training to quantify transfer and forgetting. Our results show that RFT generalizes well across task difficulty within an environment, but exhibits weaker transfer to unseen environments, which correlates with shifts in both semantic priors and observation/action interfaces. In contrast, sequential training yields promising downstream gains with minimal upstream forgetting, and mixture training across environments improves the overall balance. We further provide detailed analyses and deeper insights, and hope our work helps the community develop and deploy generalizable LLM agents.

摘要（中文）: 强化微调 (RFT) 在训练 LLM 智能体基于环境反馈执行多轮决策方面展现出潜力。然而，现有的大部分评估仍然主要局限于同一领域：训练和测试都在同一环境中甚至相同的任务上进行。在现实世界的部署中，智能体可能在具有不同背景知识、观察空间和动作界面的未知环境中运行。为了描述 RFT 在这种变化下的泛化特性，我们沿着三个维度进行了一项系统性研究：（1）环境内部，跨任务难度的泛化；（2）跨环境迁移，迁移到未知的环境；以及（3）序列化多环境训练，用于量化迁移和遗忘。我们的结果表明，RFT 在环境内部的任务难度上泛化良好，但在迁移到未知环境时表现较弱，这与语义先验和观察/动作界面的变化相关。相比之下，序列化训练产生了有希望的下游增益，且上游遗忘极小，而跨环境的混合训练提高了整体的平衡性。我们进一步提供了详细的分析和更深入的见解，并希望我们的工作能够帮助社区开发和部署可泛化的 LLM 智能体。

TLDR: This paper empirically studies the generalization capabilities of Reinforcement Fine-Tuned LLM agents across different environment shifts, revealing good generalization within environments but weaker transferability to unseen ones. Sequential training and mixture training offer promising solutions.

简要说明: 本文实证研究了强化微调的LLM智能体在不同环境变化中的泛化能力，揭示了在环境内的良好泛化，但在未见环境中的迁移能力较弱。顺序训练和混合训练提供了有希望的解决方案。

Authors: Zhiheng Xi, Xin Guo, Jiaqi Liu, Jiazheng Zhang, Yutao Fan, Zhihao Zhang, Shichun Liu, Mingxu Chai, Xiaowei Shi, Yitao Zhai, Xunliang Cai, Tao Gui, Qi Zhang, Xuanjing Huang

HomeSafe-Bench: Evaluating Vision-Language Models on Unsafe Action Detection for Embodied Agents in Household Scenarios

Abstract (English): The rapid evolution of embodied agents has accelerated the deployment of household robots in real-world environments. However, unlike structured industrial settings, household spaces introduce unpredictable safety risks, where system limitations such as perception latency and lack of common sense knowledge can lead to dangerous errors. Current safety evaluations, often restricted to static images, text, or general hazards, fail to adequately benchmark dynamic unsafe action detection in these specific contexts. To bridge this gap, we introduce \textbf{HomeSafe-Bench}, a challenging benchmark designed to evaluate Vision-Language Models (VLMs) on unsafe action detection in household scenarios. HomeSafe-Bench is contrusted via a hybrid pipeline combining physical simulation with advanced video generation and features 438 diverse cases across six functional areas with fine-grained multidimensional annotations. Beyond benchmarking, we propose \textbf{Hierarchical Dual-Brain Guard for Household Safety (HD-Guard)}, a hierarchical streaming architecture for real-time safety monitoring. HD-Guard coordinates a lightweight FastBrain for continuous high-frequency screening with an asynchronous large-scale SlowBrain for deep multimodal reasoning, effectively balancing inference efficiency with detection accuracy. Evaluations demonstrate that HD-Guard achieves a superior trade-off between latency and performance, while our analysis identifies critical bottlenecks in current VLM-based safety detection.

摘要（中文）: 具体化身载体的发展迅速，加速了家用机器人在现实世界环境中的部署。然而，与结构化的工业环境不同，家庭空间引入了不可预测的安全风险，其中系统局限性（如感知延迟和缺乏常识知识）可能导致危险错误。目前的安全评估通常局限于静态图像、文本或一般性危害，无法充分衡量在这些特定情境下对动态不安全行为的检测。为了弥合这一差距，我们引入了 \textbf{HomeSafe-Bench}，这是一个具有挑战性的基准，旨在评估视觉-语言模型 (VLMs) 在家庭场景中对不安全行为的检测能力。HomeSafe-Bench 通过结合物理模拟与高级视频生成的混合流程构建，并在六个功能区域中包含 438 个不同的案例，具有细粒度的多维标注。除了基准测试之外，我们还提出了 \textbf{用于家庭安全的层级双脑保护 (HD-Guard)}，这是一种用于实时安全监控的层级流式架构。HD-Guard 协调一个轻量级的快速脑 (FastBrain) 用于连续的高频筛查，以及一个异步的大规模慢速脑 (SlowBrain) 用于深度多模态推理，从而有效平衡了推理效率与检测精度。评估表明，HD-Guard 在延迟和性能之间取得了更出色的平衡，同时我们的分析也发现了当前基于 VLM 的安全检测中的关键瓶颈。

TLDR: The paper introduces HomeSafe-Bench, a new benchmark for evaluating Vision-Language Models on unsafe action detection in household environments, and proposes HD-Guard, a hierarchical architecture for real-time safety monitoring that balances accuracy and efficiency.

Authors: Jiayue Pu, Zhongxiang Sun, Zilu Zhang, Xiao Zhang, Jun Xu

Learning Transferable Sensor Models via Language-Informed Pretraining

Abstract (English): Modern sensing systems generate large volumes of unlabeled multivariate time-series data. This abundance of unlabeled data makes self-supervised learning (SSL) a natural approach for learning transferable representations. However, most existing approaches are optimized for reconstruction or forecasting objectives and often fail to capture the semantic structure required for downstream classification and reasoning tasks. While recent sensor-language alignment methods improve semantic generalization through captioning and zero-shot transfer, they are limited to fixed sensor configurations, such as predefined channel sets, signal lengths, or temporal resolutions, which hinders cross-domain applicability. To address these gaps, we introduce \textbf{SLIP} (\textbf{S}ensor \textbf{L}anguage-\textbf{I}nformed \textbf{P}retraining), an open-source framework for learning language-aligned representations that generalize across diverse sensor setups. SLIP integrates contrastive alignment with sensor-conditioned captioning, facilitating both discriminative understanding and generative reasoning. By repurposing a pretrained decoder-only language model via cross-attention and introducing an elegant, flexible patch-embedder, SLIP supports different temporal resolutions and variable-length input at inference time without additional retraining. Across 11 datasets, SLIP demonstrates superior performance in zero-shot transfer, signal captioning, and question answering. It achieves a 77.14% average linear-probing accuracy, a 5.93% relative improvement over strong baselines, and reaches 64.83% accuracy in sensor-based question answering.

摘要（中文）: 现代传感系统产生大量的未标注多元时间序列数据。这种未标注数据的丰富性使得自监督学习（SSL）成为学习可迁移表征的自然方法。然而，大多数现有方法针对重建或预测目标进行优化，并且通常无法捕捉下游分类和推理任务所需的语义结构。虽然最近的传感器-语言对齐方法通过字幕和零样本迁移改善了语义泛化能力，但它们仅限于固定的传感器配置，例如预定义的通道集、信号长度或时间分辨率，这阻碍了跨领域的适用性。为了解决这些差距，我们引入了 \textbf{SLIP} (\textbf{S}ensor \textbf{L}anguage-\textbf{I}nformed \textbf{P}retraining，传感器语言信息预训练)，这是一个开源框架，用于学习可以泛化到各种传感器设置的语言对齐表征。SLIP 将对比对齐与传感器条件字幕相结合，促进了判别理解和生成推理。通过使用交叉注意力重新利用预训练的仅解码器语言模型，并引入一个优雅、灵活的补丁嵌入器，SLIP 支持在推理时使用不同的时间分辨率和可变长度输入，而无需额外的再训练。在 11 个数据集上，SLIP 在零样本迁移、信号字幕和问题回答方面表现出卓越的性能。它实现了 77.14% 的平均线性探测精度，相对于强基线有 5.93% 的相对提升，并在基于传感器的问题回答中达到了 64.83% 的精度。

TLDR: The paper introduces SLIP, a framework for learning language-aligned sensor representations transferable across diverse sensor setups, using contrastive alignment and sensor-conditioned captioning with a pretrained language model. It demonstrates superior performance in zero-shot transfer, captioning, and question answering tasks across 11 datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SLIP，一个用于学习可在不同传感器设置之间迁移的语言对齐传感器表征的框架。它利用对比对齐和以传感器为条件的字幕生成，结合预训练的语言模型，并在11个数据集上展示了在零样本迁移、字幕生成和问答任务中的卓越性能。

Authors: Yuliang Chen, Arvind Pillai, Yu Yvonne Wu, Tess Z. Griffin, Lisa Marsch, Michael V. Heinz, Nicholas C. Jacobson, Andrew Campbell

Think While Watching: Online Streaming Segment-Level Memory for Multi-Turn Video Reasoning in Multimodal Large Language Models

Abstract (English): Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have shown strong performance on offline video understanding, but most are limited to offline inference or have weak online reasoning, making multi-turn interaction over continuously arriving video streams difficult. Existing streaming methods typically use an interleaved perception-generation paradigm, which prevents concurrent perception and generation and leads to early memory decay as streams grow, hurting long-range dependency modeling. We propose Think While Watching, a memory-anchored streaming video reasoning framework that preserves continuous segment-level memory during multi-turn interaction. We build a three-stage, multi-round chain-of-thought dataset and adopt a stage-matched training strategy, while enforcing strict causality through a segment-level streaming causal mask and streaming positional encoding. During inference, we introduce an efficient pipeline that overlaps watching and thinking and adaptively selects the best attention backend. Under both single-round and multi-round streaming input protocols, our method achieves strong results. Built on Qwen3-VL, it improves single-round accuracy by 2.6% on StreamingBench and by 3.79% on OVO-Bench. In the multi-round setting, it maintains performance while reducing output tokens by 56%. Code is available at: https://github.com/wl666hhh/Think_While_Watching/

摘要（中文）: 多模态大型语言模型(MLLMs)在离线视频理解方面表现出强大的性能，但是大多数模型仅限于离线推理或在线推理能力较弱，这导致对持续到达的视频流进行多轮交互变得困难。现有的流式处理方法通常使用交错的感知-生成范式，这阻碍了并发的感知和生成，并导致随着流增长，早期记忆衰减，从而损害了长程依赖建模。我们提出“边看边想”(Think While Watching)，这是一种记忆锚定的流式视频推理框架，它在多轮交互过程中保留了连续的片段级别记忆。我们构建了一个三阶段、多轮的思维链数据集，并采用了阶段匹配的训练策略，同时通过片段级别的流式因果掩码和流式位置编码来强制执行严格的因果关系。在推理过程中，我们引入了一种高效的流水线，可以重叠观看和思考过程，并自适应地选择最佳的注意力后端。在单轮和多轮流式输入协议下，我们的方法都取得了强大的结果。基于Qwen3-VL，我们的方法在StreamingBench上将单轮准确率提高了2.6%，在OVO-Bench上提高了3.79%。在多轮设置中，我们的方法可以在保持性能的同时减少56%的输出token。代码可在以下网址获得：https://github.com/wl666hhh/Think_While_Watching/

TLDR: The paper introduces Think While Watching, a memory-anchored framework for streaming video reasoning in MLLMs, addressing the limitations of existing methods with segment-level memory and a three-stage chain-of-thought dataset, achieving performance improvements on streaming video benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Think While Watching，一个用于MLLM中流式视频推理的memory-anchored框架，通过分段级别的记忆和一个三阶段的思维链数据集，解决了现有方法的局限性，并在流式视频基准测试中实现了性能提升。

Authors: Lu Wang, Zhuoran Jin, Yupu Hao, Yubo Chen, Kang Liu, Yulong Ao, Jun Zhao

You Told Me to Do It: Measuring Instructional Text-induced Private Data Leakage in LLM Agents

Abstract (English): High-privilege LLM agents that autonomously process external documentation are increasingly trusted to automate tasks by reading and executing project instructions, yet they are granted terminal access, filesystem control, and outbound network connectivity with minimal security oversight. We identify and systematically measure a fundamental vulnerability in this trust model, which we term the \emph{Trusted Executor Dilemma}: agents execute documentation-embedded instructions, including adversarial ones, at high rates because they cannot distinguish malicious directives from legitimate setup guidance. This vulnerability is a structural consequence of the instruction-following design paradigm, not an implementation bug. To structure our measurement, we formalize a three-dimensional taxonomy covering linguistic disguise, structural obfuscation, and semantic abstraction, and construct \textbf{ReadSecBench}, a benchmark of 500 real-world README files enabling reproducible evaluation. Experiments on the commercially deployed computer-use agent show end-to-end exfiltration success rates up to 85\%, consistent across five programming languages and three injection positions. Cross-model evaluation on four LLM families in a simulation environment confirms that semantic compliance with injected instructions is consistent across model families. A 15-participant user study yields a 0\% detection rate across all participants, and evaluation of 12 rule-based and 6 LLM-based defenses shows neither category achieves reliable detection without unacceptable false-positive rates. Together, these results quantify a persistent \emph{Semantic-Safety Gap} between agents' functional compliance and their security awareness, establishing that documentation-embedded instruction injection is a persistent and currently unmitigated threat to high-privilege LLM agent deployments.

摘要（中文）: 高度权限的LLM代理越来越多地被信任通过读取和执行项目指令来自动执行任务，这些代理能够自主处理外部文档，但它们在极少的安全监督下被授予终端访问权限、文件系统控制权和出站网络连接。我们识别并系统地衡量了这种信任模型中的一个根本漏洞，我们称之为“**受信任执行器困境**”：代理执行嵌入在文档中的指令，包括对抗性的指令，因为它们无法区分恶意指令和合法的设置指导，因此执行率很高。这种漏洞是指令遵循设计范式的结构性结果，而不是实现错误。为了构建我们的评估，我们形式化了一个三维分类法，涵盖语言伪装、结构混淆和语义抽象，并构建了**ReadSecBench**，这是一个包含500个真实世界README文件的基准，可以实现可重复的评估。在商业部署的计算机使用代理上的实验表明，端到端数据泄露的成功率高达85％，在五种编程语言和三个注入位置上具有一致性。在模拟环境中对四个LLM家族进行的跨模型评估证实，对注入指令的语义遵循在不同的模型家族中是一致的。一项包含15名参与者的用户研究表明，所有参与者的检测率为0％，对12个基于规则和6个基于LLM的防御措施的评估表明，没有一类能够实现可靠的检测，同时又不会产生不可接受的误报率。总之，这些结果量化了代理的功能依从性与其安全意识之间持续存在的“**语义安全差距**”，从而确定文档嵌入式指令注入是对高度权限LLM代理部署的持久且目前尚未缓解的威胁。

TLDR: This paper identifies a critical vulnerability in LLM agents: their susceptibility to malicious instructions embedded in documentation, leading to private data leakage. They quantify the problem with a new benchmark and demonstrate its persistence across models and defenses.

简要说明: 本文揭示了LLM代理中的一个关键漏洞：它们容易受到嵌入在文档中的恶意指令的影响，从而导致私有数据泄露。他们使用一个新的基准测试来量化这个问题，并证明了它在不同的模型和防御机制中持续存在。

Authors: Ching-Yu Kao, Xinfeng Li, Shenyu Dai, Tianze Qiu, Pengcheng Zhou, Eric Hanchen Jiang, Philip Sperl

From Control to Foresight: Simulation as a New Paradigm for Human-Agent Collaboration

Abstract (English): Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used to power autonomous agents for complex, multi-step tasks. However, human-agent interaction remains pointwise and reactive: users approve or correct individual actions to mitigate immediate risks, without visibility into subsequent consequences. This forces users to mentally simulate long-term effects, a cognitively demanding and often inaccurate process. Users have control over individual steps but lack the foresight to make informed decisions. We argue that effective collaboration requires foresight, not just control. We propose simulation-in-the-loop, an interaction paradigm that enables users and agents to explore simulated future trajectories before committing to decisions. Simulation transforms intervention from reactive guesswork into informed exploration, while helping users discover latent constraints and preferences along the way. This perspective paper characterizes the limitations of current paradigms, introduces a conceptual framework for simulation-based collaboration, and illustrates its potential through concrete human-agent collaboration scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLMs）正越来越多地被用于驱动自主智能体执行复杂、多步骤的任务。然而，当前人机交互仍然是点状的、被动的：用户批准或纠正个别动作以减轻即时风险，却无法洞察后续后果。这迫使用户在脑海中模拟长期影响，这是一个认知负担繁重且往往不准确的过程。用户可以控制单个步骤，但缺乏远见来做出明智的决策。我们认为，有效的协作需要远见，而不仅仅是控制。我们提出环路内模拟，这是一种交互范式，让用户和智能体能够在提交决策之前探索模拟的未来轨迹。模拟将干预从被动的猜测转变为知情的探索，同时帮助用户发现潜在的约束和偏好。这篇观点文章阐述了当前范式的局限性，介绍了基于模拟协作的概念框架，并通过具体的人机协作场景来说明其潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces simulation-in-the-loop, a new paradigm for human-agent collaboration where users explore simulated future trajectories to make informed decisions, improving foresight and reducing reliance on reactive control.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种用于人机协作的新范例：循环模拟，用户可以通过探索模拟的未来轨迹来做出明智的决策，从而提高远见性并减少对被动控制的依赖。

Authors: Gaole He, Brian Y. Lim

Tokenization Allows Multimodal Large Language Models to Understand, Generate and Edit Architectural Floor Plans

Abstract (English): Architectural floor plan design demands joint reasoning over geometry, semantics, and spatial hierarchy, which remains a major challenge for current AI systems. Although recent diffusion and language models improve visual fidelity, they still struggle with coherent spatial reasoning and controllable generation. We present HouseMind, a multimodal large language model that unifies floor plan understanding, generation, and editing in one framework. We introduce discrete room-instance tokens to construct a unified vocabulary that bridges layouts and symbolic reasoning. With multimodal alignment and instruction tuning, the model synthesizes coherent, controllable layouts from text instructions. Experiments show how the framework achieves superior geometric validity and controllability while remaining efficient and locally deployable.

摘要（中文）: 建筑平面图设计需要对几何形状、语义和空间层级结构进行联合推理，这对目前的人工智能系统来说仍然是一个主要的挑战。尽管最近的扩散模型和语言模型提高了视觉逼真度，但它们仍然难以实现连贯的空间推理和可控的生成。我们提出了HouseMind，一个多模态大型语言模型，它在一个框架中统一了平面图理解、生成和编辑。 我们引入了离散房间实例标记来构建一个统一的词汇表，连接布局和符号推理。通过多模态对齐和指令调优，该模型可以从文本指令中合成连贯、可控的布局。实验表明，该框架在保持高效和本地可部署的同时，实现了卓越的几何有效性和可控性。
