Authors: Shuo Sun, Unal Artan, Malcolm Mielle, Achim J. Lilienthaland, Martin Magnusson

MV-SAM3D: Adaptive Multi-View Fusion for Layout-Aware 3D Generation

Abstract (English): Recent unified 3D generation models have made remarkable progress in producing high-quality 3D assets from a single image. Notably, layout-aware approaches such as SAM3D can reconstruct multiple objects while preserving their spatial arrangement, opening the door to practical scene-level 3D generation. However, current methods are limited to single-view input and cannot leverage complementary multi-view observations, while independently estimated object poses often lead to physically implausible layouts such as interpenetration and floating artifacts. We present MV-SAM3D, a training-free framework that extends layout-aware 3D generation with multi-view consistency and physical plausibility. We formulate multi-view fusion as a Multi-Diffusion process in 3D latent space and propose two adaptive weighting strategies -- attention-entropy weighting and visibility weighting -- that enable confidence-aware fusion, ensuring each viewpoint contributes according to its local observation reliability. For multi-object composition, we introduce physics-aware optimization that injects collision and contact constraints both during and after generation, yielding physically plausible object arrangements. Experiments on standard benchmarks and real-world multi-object scenes demonstrate significant improvements in reconstruction fidelity and layout plausibility, all without any additional training. Code is available at https://github.com/devinli123/MV-SAM3D.

摘要（中文）: 近期统一的3D生成模型在从单张图像生成高质量3D资产方面取得了显著进展。值得注意的是，诸如SAM3D等布局感知的模型能够重建多个对象，同时保留其空间排列，为实际场景级别的3D生成打开了局面。然而，现有方法仅限于单视角输入，无法利用互补的多视角观测，并且独立估计的对象姿态常常导致物理上不合理的布局，例如物体互相穿透和悬浮伪影。 我们提出MV-SAM3D，一个无需训练的框架，将布局感知的3D生成扩展到多视角一致性和物理合理性。我们将多视角融合构建为3D潜在空间中的多重扩散过程，并提出两种自适应加权策略——注意力熵加权和可见性加权——从而实现置信度感知的融合，确保每个视角根据其局部观测的可靠性做出贡献。对于多物体组合，我们引入了物理感知优化，在生成过程中和之后注入碰撞和接触约束，从而产生物理上合理的物体排列。在标准基准和真实世界多物体场景上的实验表明，重建保真度和布局合理性都得到了显著提高，且无需任何额外的训练。代码可在https://github.com/devinli123/MV-SAM3D获取。

Authors: Baicheng Li, Dong Wu, Jun Li, Shunkai Zhou, Zecui Zeng, Lusong Li, Hongbin Zha

GGPT: Geometry Grounded Point Transformer

Abstract (English): Recent feed-forward networks have achieved remarkable progress in sparse-view 3D reconstruction by predicting dense point maps directly from RGB images. However, they often suffer from geometric inconsistencies and limited fine-grained accuracy due to the absence of explicit multi-view constraints. We introduce the Geometry-Grounded Point Transformer (GGPT), a framework that augments feed-forward reconstruction with reliable sparse geometric guidance. We first propose an improved Structure-from-Motion pipeline based on dense feature matching and lightweight geometric optimisation to efficiently estimate accurate camera poses and partial 3D point clouds from sparse input views. Building on this foundation, we propose a geometry-guided 3D point transformer that refines dense point maps under explicit partial-geometry supervision using an optimised guidance encoding. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method provides a principled mechanism for integrating geometric priors with dense feed-forward predictions, producing reconstructions that are both geometrically consistent and spatially complete, recovering fine structures and filling gaps in textureless areas. Trained solely on ScanNet++ with VGGT predictions, GGPT generalises across architectures and datasets, substantially outperforming state-of-the-art feed-forward 3D reconstruction models in both in-domain and out-of-domain settings.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 近年来，前馈神经网络在稀疏视角三维重建领域取得了显著进展，其通过直接从RGB图像预测密集点图实现重建。然而，由于缺乏显式的多视角约束，它们常常面临几何不一致性和精细粒度精度受限的问题。我们提出了几何引导点变换器（GGPT），该框架通过可靠的稀疏几何指导增强前馈重建。我们首先提出了一种改进的基于密集特征匹配和轻量几何优化的运动结构恢复流水线，以从稀疏输入视角高效估计精确的相机位姿和局部三维点云。在此基础上，我们提出了一个几何引导的三维点变换器，其利用优化的引导编码，在显式局部几何监督下细化密集点图。大量实验表明，我们的方法提供了一种将几何先验与密集前馈预测相结合的原则性机制，生成既具有几何一致性又具有空间完整性的重建结果，恢复精细结构并填补无纹理区域的间隙。GGPT仅在ScanNet++数据集上使用VGGT预测进行训练，即可跨架构和数据集进行泛化，在领域内和领域外设置中均显著优于最先进的前馈三维重建模型。

TLDR: The paper introduces GGPT, a novel framework integrating sparse geometric guidance into feed-forward 3D reconstruction using a point transformer, achieving geometrically consistent and spatially complete reconstructions with improved fine-grained accuracy and generalizability.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种名为 GGPT 的新框架，该框架使用点变换器将稀疏几何引导集成到前馈 3D 重建中，从而实现几何一致且空间完整的重建，并提高了细粒度准确性和泛化能力。

Authors: Yutong Chen, Yiming Wang, Xucong Zhang, Sergey Prokudin, Siyu Tang

Ensuring Safety in Automated Mechanical Ventilation through Offline Reinforcement Learning and Digital Twin Verification

Abstract (English): Mechanical ventilation (MV) is a life-saving intervention for patients with acute respiratory failure (ARF) in the ICU. However, inappropriate ventilator settings could cause ventilator-induced lung injury (VILI). Also, clinicians workload is shown to be directly linked to patient outcomes. Hence, MV should be personalized and automated to improve patient outcomes. Previous attempts to incorporate personalization and automation in MV include traditional supervised learning and offline reinforcement learning (RL) approaches, which often neglect temporal dependencies and rely excessively on mortality-based rewards. As a result, early stage physiological deterioration and the risk of VILI are not adequately captured. To address these limitations, we propose Transformer-based Conservative Q-Learning (T-CQL), a novel offline RL framework that integrates a Transformer encoder for effective temporal modeling of patient dynamics, conservative adaptive regularization based on uncertainty quantification to ensure safety, and consistency regularization for robust decision-making. We build a clinically informed reward function that incorporates indicators of VILI and a score for severity of patients illness. Also, previous work predominantly uses Fitted Q-Evaluation (FQE) for RL policy evaluation on static offline data, which is less responsive to dynamic environmental changes and susceptible to distribution shifts. To overcome these evaluation limitations, interactive digital twins of ARF patients were used for online "at the bedside" evaluation. Our results demonstrate that T-CQL consistently outperforms existing state-of-the-art offline RL methodologies, providing safer and more effective ventilatory adjustments. Our framework demonstrates the potential of Transformer-based models combined with conservative RL strategies as a decision support tool in critical care.

摘要（中文）: 机械通气（MV）是ICU中急性呼吸衰竭（ARF）患者的救命干预措施。然而，不适当的呼吸机设置可能导致呼吸机诱导的肺损伤（VILI）。此外，临床医生的工作量已被证明与患者的预后直接相关。因此，机械通气应该个性化和自动化，以改善患者的预后。先前在机械通气中引入个性化和自动化的尝试包括传统的监督学习和离线强化学习（RL）方法，这些方法常常忽略时间依赖性，并且过度依赖基于死亡率的奖励。因此，无法充分捕捉早期阶段的生理恶化和VILI风险。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了一种基于Transformer的保守Q学习（T-CQL），这是一种新型的离线强化学习框架，它集成了Transformer编码器以有效地对患者动态进行时间建模，基于不确定性量化的保守自适应正则化以确保安全性，以及用于稳健决策的一致性正则化。我们构建了一个临床上知情的奖励函数，其中包含VILI指标和患者病情严重程度评分。此外，先前的工作主要使用拟合Q值评估（FQE）在静态离线数据上进行RL策略评估，这种方法对动态环境变化的响应较差，且容易受到分布偏移的影响。为了克服这些评估局限性，我们使用ARF患者的交互式数字孪生体进行在线“床旁”评估。我们的结果表明，T-CQL始终优于现有的最先进的离线RL方法，提供了更安全、更有效的通气调整。我们的框架展示了基于Transformer的模型与保守RL策略相结合作为重症监护决策支持工具的潜力。

TLDR: This paper introduces Transformer-based Conservative Q-Learning (T-CQL) for automated mechanical ventilation, improving safety and effectiveness by addressing limitations of previous offline RL approaches through temporal modeling, uncertainty quantification, and digital twin verification.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了基于Transformer的保守Q学习（T-CQL）方法，用于自动化机械通气，通过解决先前离线强化学习方法的局限性（如时序建模、不确定性量化和数字孪生验证），从而提高安全性和有效性。

Authors: Hang Yu, Huidong Liu, Qingchen Zhang, William Joy, Kateryna Nikulina, Andreas A. Schuppert, Sina Saffaran, Declan Bates

abx_amr_simulator: A simulation environment for antibiotic prescribing policy optimization under antimicrobial resistance

Abstract (English): Antimicrobial resistance (AMR) poses a global health threat, reducing the effectiveness of antibiotics and complicating clinical decision-making. To address this challenge, we introduce abx_amr_simulator, a Python-based simulation package designed to model antibiotic prescribing and AMR dynamics within a controlled, reinforcement learning (RL)-compatible environment. The simulator allows users to specify patient populations, antibiotic-specific AMR response curves, and reward functions that balance immedi- ate clinical benefit against long-term resistance management. Key features include a modular design for configuring patient attributes, antibiotic resistance dynamics modeled via a leaky-balloon abstraction, and tools to explore partial observability through noise, bias, and delay in observations. The package is compatible with the Gymnasium RL API, enabling users to train and test RL agents under diverse clinical scenarios. From an ML perspective, the package provides a configurable benchmark environment for sequential decision-making under uncertainty, including partial observability induced by noisy, biased, and delayed observations. By providing a customizable and extensible framework, abx_amr_simulator offers a valuable tool for studying AMR dynamics and optimizing antibiotic stewardship strategies under realistic uncertainty.

摘要（中文）: 抗菌药物耐药性 (AMR) 构成了全球性的健康威胁，降低了抗生素的有效性并使临床决策复杂化。为了应对这一挑战，我们推出了 abx_amr_simulator，这是一个基于 Python 的模拟软件包，旨在模拟受控的、强化学习 (RL) 兼容的环境中抗生素处方和 AMR 动态。该模拟器允许用户指定患者人群、抗生素特异性 AMR 响应曲线以及在即时临床获益与长期耐药性管理之间取得平衡的奖励函数。其关键特性包括用于配置患者属性的模块化设计、通过漏气气球抽象建模的抗生素耐药性动态，以及通过观察中的噪声、偏差和延迟来探索部分可观测性的工具。该软件包与 Gymnasium RL API 兼容，使用户能够在不同的临床场景下训练和测试 RL 智能体。从机器学习的角度来看，该软件包为不确定性下的序贯决策提供了一个可配置的基准环境，包括由噪声、偏差和延迟观察引起的部分可观测性。通过提供一个可定制和可扩展的框架，abx_amr_simulator 为研究 AMR 动态以及在现实不确定性下优化抗菌药物管理策略提供了一个有价值的工具。

Authors: Joyce Lee, Seth Blumberg

CRAFT: A Tendon-Driven Hand with Hybrid Hard-Soft Compliance

Abstract (English): We introduce CRAFT hand, a tendon-driven anthropomorphic hand with hybrid hard-soft compliance for contact-rich manipulation. The design is based on a simple idea: contact is not uniform across the hand. Impacts concentrate at joints, while links carry most of the load. CRAFT places soft material at joints and keeps links rigid, and uses rollingcontact joint surfaces to keep flexion on repeatable motion paths. Fifteen motors mounted on the fingers drive the hand through tendons, keeping the form factor compact and the fingers light. In structural tests, CRAFT improves strength and endurance while maintaining comparable repeatability. In teleoperation, CRAFT improves handling of fragile and low-friction items, and the hand covers 33/33 grasps in the Feix taxonomy. The full design costs under $600 and will be released open-source with visionbased teleoperation and simulation integration. Project page: http://craft-hand.github.io/

摘要（中文）: 我们介绍CRAFT hand，一种肌腱驱动的拟人化手，采用硬-软混合顺应性设计，适用于富接触操作。其设计基于一个简单的理念：接触在手部各处并非均匀分布。冲击力集中在关节处，而连杆则承受大部分载荷。CRAFT手将软材料置于关节处，并保持连杆刚性，同时使用滚动接触的关节表面，使得屈曲沿着可重复的运动路径进行。安装在手指上的十五个电机通过肌腱驱动手，保持紧凑的外形尺寸和轻巧的手指。在结构测试中，CRAFT手在保持可比拟重复性的同时，提高了强度和耐久性。在遥操作中，CRAFT手提高了处理易碎和低摩擦物体的能力，并且该手可以完成Feix分类法中的33/33种抓取动作。完整的设计成本低于600美元，并将以开源形式发布，并提供基于视觉的遥操作和仿真集成。项目页面：http://craft-hand.github.io/

TLDR: The paper presents CRAFT, a low-cost, tendon-driven anthropomorphic hand with hybrid hard-soft compliance designed for improved strength, endurance, and precision in contact-rich manipulation, achieving a high grasp success rate and open-source availability.

简要说明: 该论文介绍CRAFT机械手，一种低成本、肌腱驱动的拟人机械手，具有混合硬软顺应性，旨在提高接触丰富操作的强度、耐用性和精度，具有很高的抓取成功率，并且是开源的。

Authors: Leo Lin, Shivansh Patel, Jay Moon, Svetlana Lazebnik, Unnat Jain

Towards Dynamic Model Identification and Gravity Compensation for the dVRK-Si Patient Side Manipulator

Abstract (English): The da Vinci Research Kit (dVRK) is widely used for research in robot-assisted surgery, but most modeling and control methods target the first-generation dVRK Classic. The recently introduced dVRK-Si, built from da Vinci Si hardware, features a redesigned Patient Side Manipulator (PSM) with substantially larger gravity loading, which can degrade control if unmodeled. This paper presents the first complete kinematic and dynamic modeling framework for the dVRK-Si PSM. We derive a modified DH kinematic model that captures the closed-chain parallelogram mechanism, formulate dynamics via the Euler-Lagrange method, and express inverse dynamics in a linear-in-parameters regressor form. Dynamic parameters are identified from data collected on a periodic excitation trajectory optimized for numerical conditioning and estimated by convex optimization with physical feasibility constraints. Using the identified model, we implement real-time gravity compensation and computed-torque feedforward in the dVRK control stack. Experiments on a physical dVRK-Si show that the gravity compensation reduces steady-state joint errors by 68-84% and decreases end-effector tip drift during static holds from 4.2 mm to 0.7 mm. Computed-torque feedforward further improves transient and position tracking accuracy. For sinusoidal trajectory tracking, computed-torque feedforward reduces position errors by 35% versus gravity-only feedforward and by 40% versus PID-only. The proposed pipeline supports reliable control, high-fidelity simulation, and learning-based automation on the dVRK-Si.

摘要（中文）: 达芬奇研究套件（dVRK）被广泛应用于机器人辅助外科研究，但大多数建模和控制方法都针对第一代dVRK Classic。最近推出的dVRK-Si基于达芬奇Si硬件构建，其特点是重新设计的患者侧机械臂（PSM）具有明显更大的重力负载，如果未建模，可能会降低控制性能。本文提出了dVRK-Si PSM的首个完整的运动学和动力学建模框架。我们推导了一个改进的DH运动学模型，以捕捉闭链平行四边形机构，通过欧拉-拉格朗日方法建立了动力学模型，并以线性参数回归器的形式表达了逆动力学。动态参数从针对数值条件优化的周期性激励轨迹上采集的数据中进行辨识，并通过具有物理可行性约束的凸优化进行估计。利用辨识的模型，我们在dVRK控制堆栈中实现了实时重力补偿和计算力矩前馈。在物理dVRK-Si上的实验表明，重力补偿将稳态关节误差降低了68-84%，并将静态保持期间的末端执行器尖端漂移从4.2毫米降低到0.7毫米。计算力矩前馈进一步提高了瞬态和位置跟踪的准确性。对于正弦轨迹跟踪，计算力矩前馈相较于仅重力前馈降低了35%的位置误差，相较于仅PID降低了40%的位置误差。所提出的流程支持dVRK-Si上的可靠控制、高保真模拟和基于学习的自动化。

TLDR: This paper presents a dynamic modeling and control framework for the dVRK-Si PSM, achieving significant improvements in gravity compensation and trajectory tracking accuracy using identified dynamic parameters and computed-torque feedforward.

简要说明: 该论文提出了dVRK-Si PSM的动态建模和控制框架，通过识别动态参数和计算扭矩前馈，在重力补偿和轨迹跟踪精度方面取得了显著改进。

Authors: Haoying Zhou, Hao Yang, Brendan Burkhart, Anton Deguet, Loris Fichera, Gregory S. Fischer, Jie Ying Wu, Peter Kazanzides

Flight through Narrow Gaps with Morphing-Wing Drones

Abstract (English): The size of a narrow gap traversable by a fixed-wing drone is limited by its wingspan. Inspired by birds, here, we enable the traversal of a gap of sub-wingspan width and height using a morphing-wing drone capable of temporarily sweeping in its wings mid-flight. This maneuver poses control challenges due to sudden lift loss during gap-passage at low flight speeds and the need for precisely timed wing-sweep actuation ahead of the gap. To address these challenges, we first develop an aerodynamic model for general wing-sweep morphing drone flight including low flight speeds and post-stall angles of attack. We integrate longitudinal drone dynamics into an optimal reference trajectory generation and Nonlinear Model Predictive Control framework with runtime adaptive costs and constraints. Validated on a 130 g wing-sweep-morphing drone, our method achieves an average altitude error of 5 cm during narrow-gap passage at forward speeds between 5 and 7 m/s, whilst enforcing fully swept wings near the gap across variable threshold distances. Trajectory analysis shows that the drone can compensate for lift loss during gap-passage by accelerating and pitching upwards ahead of the gap to an extent that differs between reference trajectory optimization objectives. We show that our strategy also allows for accurate gap passage on hardware whilst maintaining a constant forward flight speed reference and near-constant altitude.

摘要（中文）: 受固定翼无人机可通过的最窄间隙尺寸受其翼展限制的启发，本文借鉴鸟类，通过一种可在飞行中临时收缩翅膀的变形翼无人机，实现了对宽度和高度小于翼展的间隙的穿越。这种操作在低速飞行时，由于间隙穿越期间突然的升力损失，以及需要在间隙前精确计时的机翼收缩致动，带来了控制挑战。为了应对这些挑战，我们首先开发了一个通用的机翼扫描变形无人机飞行气动模型，包括低速飞行和失速后的攻角。我们将纵向无人机动力学集成到一个具有运行时自适应成本和约束的最优参考轨迹生成和非线性模型预测控制框架中。经验证，在 130 克的机翼扫描变形无人机上，我们的方法在 5 到 7 米/秒的前进速度下，窄间隙穿越期间实现了平均 5 厘米的高度误差，同时在跨越可变阈值距离的间隙附近保持完全收缩的机翼。轨迹分析表明，无人机可以通过在间隙前加速和向上倾斜，来补偿间隙穿越期间的升力损失，其程度因参考轨迹优化目标而异。我们还表明，我们的策略允许在硬件上进行精确的间隙穿越，同时保持恒定的前进飞行速度参考和接近恒定的高度。

TLDR: This paper introduces a morphing-wing drone and a nonlinear model predictive control framework for navigating narrow gaps by sweeping its wings mid-flight, validated with experimental results.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种变形翼无人机和一种非线性模型预测控制框架，用于通过在飞行中扫掠机翼来导航狭窄间隙，并通过实验结果进行了验证。

Authors: Julius Wanner, Hoang-Vu Phan, Charbel Toumieh, Dario Floreano

From Pets to Robots: MojiKit as a Data-Informed Toolkit for Affective HRI Design

Abstract (English): Designing affective behaviors for animal-inspired social robots often relies on intuition and personal experience, leading to fragmented outcomes. To provide more systematic guidance, we first coded and analyzed human-pet interaction videos, validated insights through literature and interviews, and created structured reference cards that map the design space of pet-inspired affective interactions. Building on this, we developed MojiKit, a toolkit combining reference cards, a zoomorphic robot prototype (MomoBot), and a behavior control studio. We evaluated MojiKit in co-creation workshops with 18 participants, finding that MojiKit helped them design 35 affective interaction patterns beyond their own pet experiences, while the code-free studio lowered the technical barrier and enhanced creative agency. Our contributions include the data-informed structured resource for pet-inspired affective HRI design, an integrated toolkit that bridges reference materials with hands-on prototyping, and empirical evidence showing how MojiKit empowers users to systematically create richer, more diverse affective robot behaviors.

Authors: Liwen He, Pingting Chen, Ziheng Tang, Yixiao Liu, Jihong Jeung, Teng Han, Xin Tong

Unsupervised LiDAR-Based Multi-UAV Detection and Tracking Under Extreme Sparsity

Abstract (English): Non-repetitive solid-state LiDAR scanning leads to an extremely sparse measurement regime for detecting airborne UAVs: a small quadrotor at 10-25 m typically produces only 1-2 returns per scan, which is far below the point densities assumed by most existing detection approaches and inadequate for robust multi-target data association. We introduce an unsupervised, LiDAR-only pipeline that addresses both detection and tracking without the need for labeled training data. The detector integrates range-adaptive DBSCAN clustering with a three-stage temporal consistency check and is benchmarked on real-world air-to-air flight data under eight different parameter configurations. The best setup attains 0.891 precision, 0.804 recall, and 0.63 m RMSE, and a systematic minPts sweep verifies that most scans contain at most 1-2 target points, directly quantifying the sparsity regime. For multi-target tracking, we compare deterministic Hungarian assignment with joint probabilistic data association (JPDA), each coupled with Interacting Multiple Model filtering, in four simulated scenarios with increasing levels of ambiguity. JPDA cuts identity switches by 64% with negligible impact on MOTA, demonstrating that probabilistic association is advantageous when UAV trajectories approach one another closely. A two-environment evaluation strategy, combining real-world detection with RTK-GPS ground truth and simulation-based tracking with identity-annotated ground truth, overcomes the limitations of GNSS-only evaluation at inter-UAV distances below 2 m.

摘要（中文）: 非重复固态激光雷达扫描导致探测空中无人机时产生极其稀疏的测量：一架位于10-25米的小型四旋翼飞行器通常每次扫描仅产生1-2个回波，远低于现有大多数检测方法所假设的点云密度，并且不足以实现鲁棒的多目标数据关联。我们提出了一种无监督的、仅依赖激光雷达的流程，无需标注训练数据即可实现检测和跟踪。该检测器集成了自适应距离的DBSCAN聚类以及三阶段时间一致性检查，并在八种不同参数配置下的真实空对空飞行数据上进行了基准测试。最佳设置获得了0.891的精确度、0.804的召回率和0.63米的RMSE。系统的minPts扫描验证了大多数扫描最多包含1-2个目标点，直接量化了稀疏性体制。对于多目标跟踪，我们比较了确定性的匈牙利分配算法和联合概率数据关联(JPDA)，每种算法都与交互式多模型滤波相结合，并在四种模拟场景中，随着模糊程度的增加进行比较。JPDA减少了64%的身份切换，对MOTA的影响可忽略不计，表明当无人机轨迹彼此接近时，概率关联是有优势的。一种结合真实世界检测（使用RTK-GPS真值）和基于仿真的跟踪（使用身份标注真值）的双环境评估策略，克服了仅使用GNSS评估在小于2米的无人机间距处的局限性。

TLDR: This paper introduces an unsupervised LiDAR-based pipeline for detecting and tracking multiple UAVs under extremely sparse LiDAR measurements, using range-adaptive DBSCAN and probabilistic data association, demonstrating good performance in real and simulated environments.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种基于激光雷达的无人机检测和跟踪的无监督流程，该流程适用于非常稀疏的激光雷达测量环境。它使用范围自适应的DBSCAN算法和概率数据关联方法，并在真实和模拟环境中表现出良好的性能。

Authors: Nivand Khosravi, Rodrigo Ventura, Meysam Basiri

A Generalized Theory of Load Distribution in Redundantly-actuated Robotic Systems

Abstract (English): This paper presents a generalized theory which describes how applied loads are distributed within rigid bodies handled by redundantly-actuated robotic systems composed of multiple independent closed-loop kinematic chains. The theory fully characterizes the feasible set of manipulating wrench distributions for a given resultant wrench applied to the rigid body and has important implications for the force-control of multifingered grippers, legged robots, cooperating robots, and other overconstrained mechanisms. We also derive explicit solutions to the wrench synthesis and wrench analysis problems. These solutions are computationally efficient and scale linearly with the number of applied wrenches, requiring neither numerical methods nor the inversion of large matrices. Finally, we identify significant shortcomings in current state-of-the-art approaches and propose corrections. These are supported by illustrative examples that demonstrate the advantages of the improved methods.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种广义理论，该理论描述了冗余驱动机器人系统（由多个独立的闭环运动链组成）操作的刚体内部应用载荷的分布情况。该理论完整地刻画了对于施加于刚体的给定合力wrench，可行的操作力wrench分布集合，并对多指灵巧手、腿式机器人、协作机器人和其他超约束机构的力控制具有重要意义。我们还推导出了力wrench综合问题和力wrench分析问题的显式解。这些解具有计算效率，并随所施加的力wrench数量线性增长，无需数值方法或大型矩阵求逆。最后，我们指出了当前最先进方法中的重要缺陷，并提出了修正方案。并通过示例说明来佐证改进方法的优势。

TLDR: The paper introduces a generalized theory for load distribution in redundantly-actuated robotic systems, offering computationally efficient solutions for wrench synthesis and analysis with demonstrated advantages over existing approaches.

Authors: Joshua Flight, Clément Gosselin

Real-time Rendering-based Surgical Instrument Tracking via Evolutionary Optimization

Abstract (English): Accurate and efficient tracking of surgical instruments is fundamental for Robot-Assisted Minimally Invasive Surgery. Although vision-based robot pose estimation has enabled markerless calibration without tedious physical setups, reliable tool tracking for surgical robots still remains challenging due to partial visibility and specialized articulation design of surgical instruments. Previous works in the field are usually prone to unreliable feature detections under degraded visual quality and data scarcity, whereas rendering-based methods often struggle with computational costs and suboptimal convergence. In this work, we incorporate CMA-ES, an evolutionary optimization strategy, into a versatile tracking pipeline that jointly estimates surgical instrument pose and joint configurations. Using batch rendering to efficiently evaluate multiple pose candidates in parallel, the method significantly reduces inference time and improves convergence robustness. The proposed framework further generalizes to joint angle-free and bi-manual tracking settings, making it suitable for both vision feedback control and online surgery video calibration. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that the proposed method significantly outperforms prior approaches in both accuracy and runtime.

摘要（中文）: 手术器械的精确高效跟踪是机器人辅助微创手术的基础。虽然基于视觉的机器人姿态估计已经实现了无需繁琐物理设置的无标记校准，但由于手术器械的部分可见性和特殊的关节设计，手术机器人的可靠器械跟踪仍然具有挑战性。该领域之前的工作通常容易受到视觉质量下降和数据稀缺情况下不可靠的特征检测的影响，而基于渲染的方法往往面临计算成本和次优收敛的问题。在本文中，我们将CMA-ES（一种进化优化策略）融入到一个通用的跟踪流程中，该流程联合估计手术器械的姿态和关节构型。通过使用批量渲染并行高效地评估多个姿态候选方案，该方法显著减少了推理时间和提高了收敛鲁棒性。所提出的框架进一步推广到无关节角和双手跟踪设置，使其适用于视觉反馈控制和在线手术视频校准。在合成和真实世界数据集上的大量实验表明，所提出的方法在精度和运行时间上均显著优于现有方法。

TLDR: This paper presents a real-time surgical instrument tracking method using evolutionary optimization and batch rendering, achieving improved accuracy and runtime compared to existing approaches, applicable for both vision feedback control and online surgery video calibration.

Authors: Hanyang Hu, Zekai Liang, Florian Richter, Michael C. Yip

MirrorDrift: Actuated Mirror-Based Attacks on LiDAR SLAM

Abstract (English): LiDAR SLAM provides high-accuracy localization but is fragile to point-cloud corruption because scan matching assumes geometric consistency. Prior physical attacks on LiDAR SLAM largely rely on LiDAR spoofing via external signal injection, which requires sensor-specific timing knowledge and is increasingly mitigated by modern defense mechanisms such as timing obfuscation and injection rejection. In this work, we show that specular reflection offers an injection-free alternative and demonstrate an attack, MirrorDrift, that uses an actuated planar mirror to cause ghost points in LiDAR scans and systematically bias scan-matching correspondences. MirrorDrift optimizes mirror placement, alignment, and actuation. In simulation, it increases the average pose error (APE) by 6.1x over random placement, degrading three SLAM systems to 2.29-3.31 m mean APE. In real-world experiments on a modern LiDAR with state-of-the-art interference mitigation, it induces localization errors of up to 6.03 m. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first successful SLAM-targeted attack against production-grade secure LiDARs.

摘要（中文）: 激光雷达SLAM提供高精度定位，但对点云损坏非常敏感，因为扫描匹配假设几何一致性。先前针对激光雷达SLAM的物理攻击主要依赖于通过外部信号注入的激光雷达欺骗，这需要传感器特定的时序知识，并且正日益被诸如时序混淆和注入拒绝等现代防御机制所缓解。在这项工作中，我们展示了镜面反射提供了一种无需注入的替代方案，并演示了一种攻击，MirrorDrift，它使用一个驱动的平面镜在激光雷达扫描中引起鬼影点，并系统性地偏置扫描匹配对应关系。MirrorDrift优化了镜面的放置、对齐和驱动。在仿真中，它比随机放置提高了平均位姿误差 (APE) 6.1倍，将三个SLAM系统的平均APE降至2.29-3.31米。在对具有最先进干扰抑制功能的现代激光雷达的真实世界实验中，它导致了高达6.03米的定位误差。据我们所知，这是首次针对量产级安全激光雷达的成功SLAM攻击。

TLDR: The paper presents MirrorDrift, a novel attack on LiDAR SLAM systems using an actuated mirror to inject ghost points and bias scan matching, demonstrating its effectiveness against modern, secure LiDARs in both simulation and real-world experiments.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种名为MirrorDrift的新型攻击，该攻击使用驱动镜面来向激光雷达SLAM系统注入虚假点并干扰扫描匹配。实验证明，这种攻击在模拟和现实环境中均能有效对抗现代的安全激光雷达系统。

Authors: Rokuto Nagata, Kenji Koide, Kazuma Ikeda, Ozora Sako, Shion Horie, Kentaro Yoshioka

ADMM-based Continuous Trajectory Optimization in Graphs of Convex Sets

Abstract (English): This paper presents a numerical solver for computing continuous trajectories in non-convex environments. Our approach relies on a customized implementation of the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM) built upon two key components: First, we parameterize trajectories as polynomials, allowing the primal update to be computed in closed form as a minimum-control-effort problem. Second, we introduce the concept of a spatio-temporal allocation graph based on a mixed-integer formulation and pose the slack update as a shortest-path search. The combination of these ingredients results in a solver with several distinct advantages over the state of the art. By jointly optimizing over both discrete spatial and continuous temporal domains, our method accesses a larger search space than existing decoupled approaches, enabling the discovery of superior trajectories. Additionally, the solver's structural robustness ensures reliable convergence from naive initializations, removing the bottleneck of complex warm starting in non-convex environments.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种用于计算非凸环境中连续轨迹的数值求解器。我们的方法依赖于一种基于交替方向乘子法(ADMM)的定制实现，该实现建立在两个关键组成部分之上：首先，我们将轨迹参数化为多项式，从而允许将原始变量更新计算为闭式形式的最小控制量问题。其次，我们引入了基于混合整数规划的时空分配图的概念，并将松弛变量更新构建为最短路径搜索。这些要素的结合使得该求解器相对于现有技术具有几个明显的优势。通过联合优化离散空间和连续时间域，我们的方法访问比现有解耦方法更大的搜索空间，从而能够发现更优的轨迹。此外，该求解器的结构鲁棒性确保了从简单初始化的可靠收敛，消除了非凸环境中复杂热启动的瓶颈。

TLDR: This paper introduces an ADMM-based solver for continuous trajectory optimization in non-convex environments, combining polynomial trajectory parameterization and a spatio-temporal allocation graph for improved performance and robustness compared to state-of-the-art methods.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于ADMM的求解器，用于在非凸环境中进行连续轨迹优化。该方法结合了多项式轨迹参数化和时空分配图，与最先进的方法相比，性能和鲁棒性有所提高。

Authors: Lukas Pries, Jon Arrizabalaga, Zachary Manchester, Markus Ryll

Distributed Kalman--Consensus Filtering with Adaptive Uncertainty Weighting for Multi-Object Tracking in Mobile Robot Networks

Abstract (English): This paper presents an implementation and evaluation of a Distributed Kalman--Consensus Filter (DKCF) for Multi-Object Tracking (MOT) in mobile robot networks operating under partial observability and heterogeneous localization uncertainty. A key challenge in such systems is the fusion of information from agents with differing localization quality, where frame misalignment can lead to inconsistent estimates, track duplication, and ghost tracks. To address this issue, we build upon the MOTLEE framework and retain its frame-alignment methodology, which uses consistently tracked dynamic objects as transient landmarks to improve relative pose estimates between robots. On top of this framework, we propose an uncertainty-aware adaptive consensus weighting mechanism that dynamically adjusts the influence of neighbor information based on the covariance of the transmitted estimates, thereby reducing the impact of unreliable data during distributed fusion. Local tracking is performed using a Kalman Filter (KF) with a Constant Velocity Model (CVM) and Global Nearest Neighbor (GNN) data association. simulation results demonstrate that adaptive weighting effectively protects local estimates from inconsistent data, yielding a MOTA improvement of 0.09 for agents suffering from localization drift, although system performance remains constrained by communication latency.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种分布式卡尔曼-一致性滤波器(DKCF)的实现与评估，用于在部分可观测性和异构定位不确定性下运行的移动机器人网络中的多目标跟踪(MOT)。此类系统中的一个关键挑战是如何融合来自定位质量不同的智能体的信息，其中帧未对齐可能导致不一致的估计、轨迹重复和幽灵轨迹。为了解决这个问题，我们在MOTLEE框架的基础上，保留了其帧对齐方法，该方法使用一致跟踪的动态对象作为瞬态地标来改进机器人之间的相对位姿估计。在此框架之上，我们提出了一种不确定性感知的自适应一致性加权机制，该机制基于所传输估计的协方差动态调整邻域信息的影响，从而减少分布式融合过程中不可靠数据的影响。局部跟踪使用具有恒定速度模型(CVM)的卡尔曼滤波器(KF)和全局最近邻(GNN)数据关联。仿真结果表明，自适应加权有效地保护了局部估计免受不一致数据的影响，对于遭受定位漂移的智能体，MOTA提高了0.09，但系统性能仍受到通信延迟的限制。

TLDR: The paper presents a Distributed Kalman--Consensus Filter with adaptive uncertainty weighting for multi-object tracking in mobile robot networks, addressing the challenge of inconsistent estimates due to differing localization quality among agents. They show MOTA improvement for agents with localization drift.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种具有自适应不确定性加权的分布式卡尔曼-共识滤波器，用于移动机器人网络中的多目标跟踪，解决了由于代理之间不同的定位质量而导致的不一致估计的挑战。 结果表明，对于具有定位漂移的代理，MOTA有所提高。

Authors: Niusha Khosravi, Rodrigo Ventura, Meysam Basiri

Multi-Robot Multitask Gaussian Process Estimation and Coverage

Abstract (English): Coverage control is essential for the optimal deployment of agents to monitor or cover areas with sensory demands. While traditional coverage involves single-task robots, increasing autonomy now enables multitask operations. This paper introduces a novel multitask coverage problem and addresses it for both the cases of known and unknown sensory demands. For known demands, we design a federated multitask coverage algorithm and establish its convergence properties. For unknown demands, we employ a multitask Gaussian Process (GP) framework to learn sensory demand functions and integrate it with the multitask coverage algorithm to develop an adaptive algorithm. We introduce a novel notion of multitask coverage regret that compares the performance of the adaptive algorithm against an oracle with prior knowledge of the demand functions. We establish that our algorithm achieves sublinear cumulative regret, and numerically illustrate its performance.

摘要（中文）: 覆盖控制对于优化部署智能体以监测或覆盖具有感觉需求的区域至关重要。 传统的覆盖范围涉及单任务机器人，而自主性的提高现在可以实现多任务操作。 本文介绍了一种新颖的多任务覆盖问题，并针对已知和未知感觉需求的情况进行了解决。 对于已知需求，我们设计了一种联合多任务覆盖算法，并建立了其收敛性。 对于未知需求，我们采用多任务高斯过程 (GP) 框架来学习感觉需求函数，并将其与多任务覆盖算法相结合，开发了一种自适应算法。 我们引入了一种新的多任务覆盖遗憾概念，该概念将自适应算法的性能与事先了解需求函数的预言机进行比较。 我们证明了我们的算法实现了次线性累积遗憾，并通过数值实验说明了其性能。

TLDR: This paper proposes a multitask coverage algorithm for multi-robot systems, addressing both known and unknown sensory demand scenarios using Gaussian Processes for learning unknown demands and establishing sublinear regret bounds for the adaptive algorithm.

Authors: Lai Wei, Andrew McDonald, Vaibhav Srivastava

A Robust and Efficient Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Framework for Traffic Signal Control

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning (RL) in Traffic Signal Control (TSC) faces significant hurdles in real-world deployment due to limited generalization to dynamic traffic flow variations. Existing approaches often overfit static patterns and use action spaces incompatible with driver expectations. This paper proposes a robust Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) framework validated in the Vissim traffic simulator. The framework integrates three mechanisms: (1) Turning Ratio Randomization, a training strategy that exposes agents to dynamic turning probabilities to enhance robustness against unseen scenarios; (2) a stability-oriented Exponential Phase Duration Adjustment action space, which balances responsiveness and precision through cyclical, exponential phase adjustments; and (3) a Neighbor-Based Observation scheme utilizing the MAPPO algorithm with Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE). By leveraging centralized updates, this approach approximates the efficacy of global observations while maintaining scalable local communication. Experimental results demonstrate that our framework outperforms standard RL baselines, reducing average waiting time by over 10%. The proposed model exhibits superior generalization in unseen traffic scenarios and maintains high control stability, offering a practical solution for adaptive signal control.

摘要（中文）: 针对交通信号控制（TSC）中的强化学习（RL）而言，由于对动态交通流量变化的泛化能力有限，实际部署面临着显著挑战。现有方法通常过度拟合静态模式，并且采用与驾驶员期望不符的动作空间。本文提出了一种鲁棒的多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架，已在Vissim交通模拟器中验证。该框架集成了三种机制：（1）转向率随机化，一种训练策略，使智能体暴露于动态转向概率，以提高对未见场景的鲁棒性；（2）面向稳定性的指数阶段时长调整动作空间，通过周期性的指数阶段调整平衡响应性和精度；以及（3）基于邻居的观测方案，利用具有集中式训练与分散式执行（CTDE）的MAPPO算法。通过利用集中式更新，这种方法在保持可扩展的局部通信的同时，近似于全局观测的有效性。实验结果表明，我们的框架优于标准的RL基线，平均等待时间减少了超过10%。所提出的模型在未见交通场景中表现出卓越的泛化能力，并保持了较高的控制稳定性，为自适应信号控制提供了一种实用的解决方案。

TLDR: This paper presents a robust MARL framework for traffic signal control, using turning ratio randomization, an exponential phase duration adjustment action space, and a neighbor-based observation scheme with MAPPO to improve generalization and reduce waiting times.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种鲁棒的多智能体强化学习框架，用于交通信号控制。该框架通过转向比随机化、指数相位时长调整动作空间和基于邻居的观测方案（使用MAPPO），提高了泛化能力并减少了等待时间。

Authors: Sheng-You Huang, Hsiao-Chuan Chang, Yen-Chi Chen, Ting-Han Wei, I-Hau Yeh, Sheng-Yao Kuan, Chien-Yao Wang, Hsuan-Han Lee, I-Chen Wu

Normative Common Ground Replication (NormCoRe): Replication-by-Translation for Studying Norms in Multi-agent AI

Abstract (English): In the late 2010s, the fashion trend NormCore framed sameness as a signal of belonging, illustrating how norms emerge through collective coordination. Today, similar forms of normative coordination can be observed in systems based on Multi-agent Artificial Intelligence (MAAI), as AI-based agents deliberate, negotiate, and converge on shared decisions in fairness-sensitive domains. Yet, existing empirical approaches often treat norms as targets for alignment or replication, implicitly assuming equivalence between human subjects and AI agents and leaving collective normative dynamics insufficiently examined. To address this gap, we propose Normative Common Ground Replication (NormCoRe), a novel methodological framework to systematically translate the design of human subject experiments into MAAI environments. Building on behavioral science, replication research, and state-of-the-art MAAI architectures, NormCoRe maps the structural layers of human subject studies onto the design of AI agent studies, enabling systematic documentation of study design and analysis of norms in MAAI. We demonstrate the utility of NormCoRe by replicating a seminal experimental study on distributive justice, in which participants negotiate fairness principles under a "veil of ignorance". We show that normative judgments in AI agent studies can differ from human baselines and are sensitive to the choice of the foundation model and the language used to instantiate agent personas. Our work provides a principled pathway for analyzing norms in MAAI and helps to guide, reflect, and document design choices whenever AI agents are used to automate or support tasks formerly carried out by humans.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 在2010年代后期，NormCore时尚潮流将趋同性视为归属感的标志，阐释了规范如何通过集体协调而涌现。如今，类似的规范性协调形式也可见于基于多智能体人工智能（MAAI）的系统中，人工智能体在公平敏感领域进行审议、协商，并就共同决策达成一致。然而，现有的经验方法通常将规范视为对齐或复制的目标，隐含地假设人类受试者和人工智能体之间是等价的，从而导致集体规范动态未得到充分考察。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出了规范性共同基础复制（NormCoRe），这是一种新颖的方法论框架，用于系统地将人类受试者实验的设计转化为MAAI环境。NormCoRe立足于行为科学、复制研究和最先进的MAAI架构，将人类受试者研究的结构层映射到人工智能体研究的设计中，从而能够系统地记录研究设计并分析MAAI中的规范。我们通过复制一项关于分配正义的开创性实验研究来展示NormCoRe的效用，在该研究中，参与者在“无知之幕”下协商公平原则。我们表明，人工智能体研究中的规范性判断可能与人类基线不同，并且对基础模型的选择以及用于实例化智能体角色的语言非常敏感。我们的工作为分析MAAI中的规范提供了一条原则性的途径，并有助于指导、反思和记录设计选择，无论何时使用人工智能体来自动化或支持以前由人类执行的任务。

TLDR: This paper introduces NormCoRe, a methodology for replicating human subject experiments in multi-agent AI environments to study normative behavior, demonstrating its use with a replication of a distributive justice experiment.

Authors: Luca Deck, Simeon Allmendinger, Lucas Müller, Niklas Kühl

Social, Legal, Ethical, Empathetic and Cultural Norm Operationalisation for AI Agents

Abstract (English): As AI agents are increasingly used in high-stakes domains like healthcare and law enforcement, aligning their behaviour with social, legal, ethical, empathetic, and cultural (SLEEC) norms has become a critical engineering challenge. While international frameworks have established high-level normative principles for AI, a significant gap remains in translating these abstract principles into concrete, verifiable requirements. To address this gap, we propose a systematic SLEEC-norm operationalisation process for determining, validating, implementing, and verifying normative requirements. Furthermore, we survey the landscape of methods and tools supporting this process, and identify key remaining challenges and research avenues for addressing them. We thus establish a framework - and define a research and policy agenda - for developing AI agents that are not only functionally useful but also demonstrably aligned with human norms and values.

摘要（中文）: 随着人工智能代理在医疗保健和执法等高风险领域中日益普及，使其行为与社会、法律、伦理、共情和文化（SLEEC）规范相符已成为一项关键的工程挑战。尽管国际框架已经为人工智能制定了高级别的规范性原则，但在将这些抽象原则转化为具体、可验证的要求方面仍然存在显著差距。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出了一种系统性的 SLEEC 规范操作化过程，用于确定、验证、实施和验证规范性要求。此外，我们调查了支持该过程的方法和工具，并确定了解决这些挑战所面临的关键难题和研究方向。因此，我们建立了一个框架，并定义了一个研究和政策议程，旨在开发不仅在功能上有用，而且在实践中与人类规范和价值观保持一致的人工智能代理。

Authors: Radu Calinescu, Ana Cavalcanti, Marsha Chechik, Lina Marsso, Beverley Townsend

How Intelligence Emerges: A Minimal Theory of Dynamic Adaptive Coordination

Abstract (English): This paper develops a dynamical theory of adaptive coordination in multi-agent systems. Rather than analyzing coordination through equilibrium optimization or agent-centric learning alone, the framework models agents, incentives, and environment as a recursively closed feedback architecture. A persistent environment stores accumulated coordination signals, a distributed incentive field transmits those signals locally, and adaptive agents update in response. Coordination is thus treated as a structural property of coupled dynamics rather than as the solution to a centralized objective. The paper establishes three structural results. First, under dissipativity assumptions, the induced closed-loop system admits a bounded forward-invariant region, ensuring viability without requiring global optimality. Second, when incentive signals depend non-trivially on persistent environmental memory, the resulting dynamics generically cannot be reduced to a static global objective defined solely over the agent state space. Third, persistent environmental state induces history sensitivity unless the system is globally contracting. A minimal linear specification illustrates how coupling, persistence, and dissipation govern local stability and oscillatory regimes through spectral conditions on the Jacobian. The results establish structural conditions under which intelligent coordination dynamics emerge from incentive-mediated adaptive interaction within a persistent environment, without presuming welfare maximization, rational expectations, or centralized design.

摘要（中文）: 本文发展了一种多智能体系统中自适应协调的动力学理论。该框架并非仅仅通过均衡优化或以智能体为中心的学习来分析协调，而是将智能体、激励和环境建模为一个递归封闭的反馈架构。一个持久环境存储积累的协调信号，一个分布式激励场在局部传递这些信号，而自适应智能体则做出响应更新。因此，协调被视为耦合动力学的一个结构属性，而不是集中式目标的解决方案。 本文确立了三个结构性结果。首先，在耗散性假设下，诱导的闭环系统容许一个有界的正向不变区域，从而保证了可行性，而无需全局最优性。其次，当激励信号非平凡地依赖于持久环境记忆时，由此产生的动力学通常不能被简化为仅在智能体状态空间上定义的静态全局目标。第三，除非系统是全局收缩的，否则持久环境状态会导致历史敏感性。 一个最小线性规范说明耦合、持久性和耗散性如何通过雅可比矩阵的谱条件来控制局部稳定性和振荡机制。这些结果确立了在持久环境中，智能协调动力学如何从激励介导的自适应交互中涌现的结构性条件，而无需假定福利最大化、理性预期或集中式设计。

TLDR: The paper presents a dynamical systems approach to modeling adaptive coordination in multi-agent systems, emphasizing the role of environmental memory and local incentives in the emergence of intelligent coordination without global optimization.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种动力系统方法，用于建模多智能体系统中的自适应协调，强调环境记忆和局部激励在智能协调涌现中的作用，无需全局优化。

Authors: Stefano Grassi

Real-World Point Tracking with Verifier-Guided Pseudo-Labeling

Abstract (English): Models for long-term point tracking are typically trained on large synthetic datasets. The performance of these models degrades in real-world videos due to different characteristics and the absence of dense ground-truth annotations. Self-training on unlabeled videos has been explored as a practical solution, but the quality of pseudo-labels strongly depends on the reliability of teacher models, which vary across frames and scenes. In this paper, we address the problem of real-world fine-tuning and introduce verifier, a meta-model that learns to assess the reliability of tracker predictions and guide pseudo-label generation. Given candidate trajectories from multiple pretrained trackers, the verifier evaluates them per frame and selects the most trustworthy predictions, resulting in high-quality pseudo-label trajectories. When applied for fine-tuning, verifier-guided pseudo-labeling substantially improves the quality of supervision and enables data-efficient adaptation to unlabeled videos. Extensive experiments on four real-world benchmarks demonstrate that our approach achieves state-of-the-art results while requiring less data than prior self-training methods. Project page: https://kuis-ai.github.io/track_on_r

摘要（中文）: 长期点跟踪模型通常在大规模合成数据集上进行训练。由于不同特性的存在以及缺乏密集的真值标注，这些模型在真实世界视频中的性能会下降。在无标签视频上进行自训练已被探索为一种可行的解决方案，但伪标签的质量强烈依赖于教师模型的可靠性，而这种可靠性在不同帧和场景之间变化。在本文中，我们解决了真实世界微调的问题，并引入了一个验证器，这是一个元模型，它学习评估跟踪器预测的可靠性并指导伪标签生成。给定来自多个预训练跟踪器的候选轨迹，验证器逐帧评估它们，并选择最可信的预测，从而产生高质量的伪标签轨迹。当应用于微调时，验证器引导的伪标签显著提高了监督的质量，并使得能够高效地适应无标签视频。在四个真实世界基准上的大量实验表明，我们的方法在需要比之前的自训练方法更少的数据的情况下，实现了最先进的结果。项目主页：https://kuis-ai.github.io/track_on_r

TLDR: The paper introduces a verifier meta-model that assesses the reliability of tracker predictions to generate high-quality pseudo-labels for self-training long-term point tracking models on real-world videos. It achieves state-of-the-art results with improved data efficiency.

Authors: Görkay Aydemir, Fatma Güney, Weidi Xie

Single Pixel Image Classification using an Ultrafast Digital Light Projector

Abstract (English): Pattern recognition and image classification are essential tasks in machine vision. Autonomous vehicles, for example, require being able to collect the complex information contained in a changing environment and classify it in real time. Here, we experimentally demonstrate image classification at multi-kHz frame rates combining the technique of single pixel imaging (SPI) with a low complexity machine learning model. The use of a microLED-on-CMOS digital light projector for SPI enables ultrafast pattern generation for sub-ms image encoding. We investigate the classification accuracy of our experimental system against the broadly accepted benchmarking task of the MNIST digits classification. We compare the classification performance of two machine learning models: An extreme learning machine (ELM) and a backpropagation trained deep neural network. The complexity of both models is kept low so the overhead added to the inference time is comparable to the image generation time. Crucially, our single pixel image classification approach is based on a spatiotemporal transformation of the information, entirely bypassing the need for image reconstruction. By exploring the performance of our SPI based ELM as binary classifier we demonstrate its potential for efficient anomaly detection in ultrafast imaging scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 模式识别和图像分类是机器视觉中的关键任务。例如，自动驾驶车辆需要能够收集不断变化的环境中包含的复杂信息，并实时对其进行分类。在这里，我们通过实验演示了结合单像素成像 (SPI) 技术和低复杂度机器学习模型，以多kHz帧率进行图像分类。使用基于CMOS的微型LED数字光投影仪进行SPI，可以实现用于亚毫秒级图像编码的超快模式生成。我们针对广泛接受的MNIST数字分类基准测试任务，研究了我们实验系统的分类准确率。我们比较了两种机器学习模型的分类性能：极限学习机 (ELM) 和反向传播训练的深度神经网络。两种模型的复杂度都保持较低水平，因此添加到推理时间的开销与图像生成时间相当。至关重要的是，我们的单像素图像分类方法基于信息的时空变换，完全绕过了图像重建的需求。通过探索我们基于SPI的ELM作为二元分类器的性能，我们证明了其在超快成像场景中用于高效异常检测的潜力。

TLDR: This paper presents a single-pixel imaging system using a digital light projector and low-complexity machine learning (ELM and DNN) for ultrafast (multi-kHz) image classification, bypassing image reconstruction, and demonstrating anomaly detection potential on MNIST.

Authors: Aisha Kanwal, Graeme E. Johnstone, Fahimeh Dehkhoda, Johannes H. Herrnsdorf, Robert K. Henderson, Martin D. Dawson, Xavier Porte, Michael J. Strain

CEI-3D: Collaborative Explicit-Implicit 3D Reconstruction for Realistic and Fine-Grained Object Editing

Abstract (English): Existing 3D editing methods often produce unrealistic and unrefined results due to the deeply integrated nature of their reconstruction networks. To address the challenge, this paper introduces CEI-3D, an editing-oriented reconstruction pipeline designed to facilitate realistic and fine-grained editing. Specifically, we propose a collaborative explicit-implicit reconstruction approach, which represents the target object using an implicit SDF network and a differentially sampled, locally controllable set of handler points. The implicit network provides a smooth and continuous geometry prior, while the explicit handler points offer localized control, enabling mutual guidance between the global 3D structure and user-specified local editing regions. To independently control each attribute of the handler points, we design a physical properties disentangling module to decouple the color of the handler points into separate physical properties. We also propose a dual-diffuse-albedo network in this module to process the edited and non-edited regions through separate branches, thereby preventing undesired interference from editing operations. Building on the reconstructed collaborative explicit-implicit representation with disentangled properties, we introduce a spatial-aware editing module that enables part-wise adjustment of relevant handler points. This module employs a cross-view propagation-based 3D segmentation strategy, which helps users to edit the specified physical attributes of a target part efficiently. Extensive experiments on both real and synthetic datasets demonstrate that our approach achieves more realistic and fine-grained editing results than the state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods while requiring less editing time. Our code is available on https://github.com/shiyue001/CEI-3D.

摘要（中文）: 现有3D编辑方法由于其重建网络的深度集成特性，往往产生不真实且粗糙的结果。为了解决这一挑战，本文提出了一种面向编辑的重建流水线CEI-3D，旨在促进真实且精细的编辑。具体而言，我们提出了一种协作式显式-隐式重建方法，该方法使用隐式SDF网络和一组可微采样、局部可控的处理点来表示目标对象。隐式网络提供平滑且连续的几何先验，而显式处理点提供局部控制，从而实现全局3D结构和用户指定的局部编辑区域之间的相互引导。为了独立控制处理点的每个属性，我们设计了一个物理属性解耦模块，将处理点的颜色解耦为独立的物理属性。我们还在该模块中提出了一个双重漫反射-反照率网络，通过单独的分支处理编辑和非编辑区域，从而防止编辑操作产生不必要的干扰。基于具有解耦属性的重建协作式显式-隐式表示，我们引入了一个空间感知编辑模块，该模块能够对相关处理点进行分部分调整。该模块采用基于跨视图传播的3D分割策略，帮助用户高效地编辑目标部分的指定物理属性。在真实和合成数据集上的大量实验表明，与最先进（SOTA）的方法相比，我们的方法实现了更加真实和精细的编辑结果，同时所需的编辑时间更少。我们的代码已在https://github.com/shiyue001/CEI-3D上提供。

TLDR: The paper introduces CEI-3D, a collaborative explicit-implicit 3D reconstruction method for realistic and fine-grained object editing, using an SDF network and handler points with disentangled physical properties. It outperforms SOTA methods in editing quality and efficiency.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CEI-3D，一种用于真实和细粒度对象编辑的协同显式-隐式3D重建方法，它使用SDF网络和具有解耦物理属性的处理点。在编辑质量和效率方面优于SOTA方法。

Authors: Yue Shi, Rui Shi, Yuxuan Xiong, Bingbing Ni, Wenjun Zhang

R4Det: 4D Radar-Camera Fusion for High-Performance 3D Object Detection

Abstract (English): 4D radar-camera sensing configuration has gained increasing importance in autonomous driving. However, existing 3D object detection methods that fuse 4D Radar and camera data confront several challenges. First, their absolute depth estimation module is not robust and accurate enough, leading to inaccurate 3D localization. Second, the performance of their temporal fusion module will degrade dramatically or even fail when the ego vehicle's pose is missing or inaccurate. Third, for some small objects, the sparse radar point clouds may completely fail to reflect from their surfaces. In such cases, detection must rely solely on visual unimodal priors. To address these limitations, we propose R4Det, which enhances depth estimation quality via the Panoramic Depth Fusion module, enabling mutual reinforcement between absolute and relative depth. For temporal fusion, we design a Deformable Gated Temporal Fusion module that does not rely on the ego vehicle's pose. In addition, we built an Instance-Guided Dynamic Refinement module that extracts semantic prototypes from 2D instance guidance. Experiments show that R4Det achieves state-of-the-art 3D object detection results on the TJ4DRadSet and VoD datasets.

摘要（中文）: 4D雷达-相机传感配置在自动驾驶领域日益重要。然而，现有的融合4D雷达和相机数据的3D目标检测方法面临着若干挑战。首先，它们的绝对深度估计模块不够鲁棒和准确，导致3D定位不精确。其次，当自车位姿缺失或不准确时，它们的时间融合模块的性能会急剧下降甚至失效。第三，对于一些小型物体，稀疏的雷达点云可能完全无法反射到其表面。在这种情况下，检测必须完全依赖视觉单模态先验。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了R4Det，它通过全景深度融合模块增强了深度估计质量，实现了绝对深度和相对深度之间的相互加强。在时间融合方面，我们设计了一个不依赖自车位姿的可变形门控时间融合模块。此外，我们构建了一个实例引导的动态细化模块，从2D实例指导中提取语义原型。实验结果表明，R4Det在TJ4DRadSet和VoD数据集上实现了最先进的3D目标检测结果。

TLDR: R4Det proposes a novel 4D radar-camera fusion method for 3D object detection in autonomous driving, enhancing depth estimation and temporal fusion while addressing limitations of existing approaches, achieving state-of-the-art results.

Authors: Zhongyu Xia, Yousen Tang, Yongtao Wang, Zhifeng Wang, Weijun Qin

Mango-GS: Enhancing Spatio-Temporal Consistency in Dynamic Scenes Reconstruction using Multi-Frame Node-Guided 4D Gaussian Splatting

Abstract (English): Reconstructing dynamic 3D scenes with photorealistic detail and strong temporal coherence remains a significant challenge. Existing Gaussian splatting approaches for dynamic scene modeling often rely on per-frame optimization, which can overfit to instantaneous states instead of capturing underlying motion dynamics. To address this, we present Mango-GS, a multi-frame, node-guided framework for high-fidelity 4D reconstruction. Mango-GS leverages a temporal Transformer to model motion dependencies within a short window of frames, producing temporally consistent deformations. For efficiency, temporal modeling is confined to a sparse set of control nodes. Each node is represented by a decoupled canonical position and a latent code, providing a stable semantic anchor for motion propagation and preventing correspondence drift under large motion. Our framework is trained end-to-end, enhanced by an input masking strategy and two multi-frame losses to improve robustness. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Mango-GS achieves state-of-the-art reconstruction quality and real-time rendering speed, enabling high-fidelity reconstruction and interactive rendering of dynamic scenes.

摘要（中文）: 重建具有照片级真实细节和强大时间一致性的动态 3D 场景仍然是一个重大挑战。现有的用于动态场景建模的高斯溅射方法通常依赖于逐帧优化，这可能会过拟合到瞬时状态，而不是捕捉潜在的运动动态。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了 Mango-GS，一种多帧、节点引导的框架，用于高保真 4D 重建。Mango-GS 利用时间 Transformer 来建模短时间内帧内的运动依赖性，从而产生时间上一致的形变。为了提高效率，时间建模被限制在一组稀疏的控制节点上。每个节点由一个解耦的规范位置和一个潜在代码表示，为运动传播提供了一个稳定的语义锚点，并防止在大运动下出现对应关系漂移。我们的框架经过端到端训练，并通过输入掩码策略和两个多帧损失进行增强，以提高鲁棒性。大量实验表明，Mango-GS 实现了最先进的重建质量和实时渲染速度，从而实现了动态场景的高保真重建和交互式渲染。

TLDR: Mango-GS introduces a novel multi-frame, node-guided 4D Gaussian Splatting framework for dynamic scene reconstruction, achieving state-of-the-art quality and real-time rendering by using a temporal Transformer and sparse control nodes to improve temporal coherence.

简要说明: Mango-GS 提出了一种新颖的多帧、节点引导的 4D 高斯溅射框架，用于动态场景重建，通过使用时间 Transformer 和稀疏控制节点来提高时间一致性，从而实现了最先进的质量和实时渲染。

Authors: Tingxuan Huang, Haowei Zhu, Jun-hai Yong, Hao Pan, Bin Wang

Mobile-GS: Real-time Gaussian Splatting for Mobile Devices

Abstract (English): 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has emerged as a powerful representation for high-quality rendering across a wide range of applications.However, its high computational demands and large storage costs pose significant challenges for deployment on mobile devices. In this work, we propose a mobile-tailored real-time Gaussian Splatting method, dubbed Mobile-GS, enabling efficient inference of Gaussian Splatting on edge devices. Specifically, we first identify alpha blending as the primary computational bottleneck, since it relies on the time-consuming Gaussian depth sorting process. To solve this issue, we propose a depth-aware order-independent rendering scheme that eliminates the need for sorting, thereby substantially accelerating rendering. Although this order-independent rendering improves rendering speed, it may introduce transparency artifacts in regions with overlapping geometry due to the scarcity of rendering order. To address this problem, we propose a neural view-dependent enhancement strategy, enabling more accurate modeling of view-dependent effects conditioned on viewing direction, 3D Gaussian geometry, and appearance attributes. In this way, Mobile-GS can achieve both high-quality and real-time rendering. Furthermore, to facilitate deployment on memory-constrained mobile platforms, we also introduce first-order spherical harmonics distillation, a neural vector quantization technique, and a contribution-based pruning strategy to reduce the number of Gaussian primitives and compress the 3D Gaussian representation with the assistance of neural networks. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our proposed Mobile-GS achieves real-time rendering and compact model size while preserving high visual quality, making it well-suited for mobile applications.

摘要（中文）: 3D高斯溅射(3DGS)已成为一种强大的表示方法，可在各种应用中实现高质量渲染。然而，其高计算需求和巨大的存储成本对移动设备上的部署提出了重大挑战。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种针对移动设备的实时高斯溅射方法，称为Mobile-GS，可在边缘设备上有效推断高斯溅射。具体而言，我们首先将Alpha混合确定为主要的计算瓶颈，因为它依赖于耗时的高斯深度排序过程。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种深度感知的与顺序无关的渲染方案，该方案消除了排序的必要性，从而大大加快了渲染速度。虽然这种与顺序无关的渲染提高了渲染速度，但由于渲染顺序的稀缺性，它可能会在具有重叠几何体的区域中引入透明伪影。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种神经视角相关的增强策略，能够更准确地建模依赖于视角方向、3D高斯几何体和外观属性的视角相关效果。通过这种方式，Mobile-GS可以实现高质量和实时的渲染。此外，为了方便在内存受限的移动平台上部署，我们还引入了一阶球谐函数蒸馏、一种神经向量量化技术和一种基于贡献的剪枝策略，以在神经网络的辅助下减少高斯基元的数量并压缩3D高斯表示。大量实验表明，我们提出的Mobile-GS实现了实时渲染和紧凑的模型尺寸，同时保持了高视觉质量，使其非常适合移动应用。

TLDR: The paper introduces Mobile-GS, a real-time 3D Gaussian Splatting method optimized for mobile devices, addressing computational bottlenecks and storage limitations through depth-aware rendering, neural view-dependent enhancement, and compression techniques.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Mobile-GS，一种针对移动设备优化的实时3D高斯溅射方法，通过深度感知渲染、神经视角依赖增强和压缩技术来解决计算瓶颈和存储限制。

Authors: Xiaobiao Du, Yida Wang, Kun Zhan, Xin Yu

Towards Automated Initial Probe Placement in Transthoracic Teleultrasound Using Human Mesh and Skeleton Recovery

Abstract (English): Cardiac and lung ultrasound are technically demanding because operators must identify patient-specific intercostal acoustic windows and then navigate between standard views by adjusting probe position, rotation, and force across different imaging planes. These challenges are amplified in teleultrasound when a novice or robot faces the difficult task of first placing the probe on the patient without in-person expert assistance. We present a framework for automating Patient registration and anatomy-informed Initial Probe placement Guidance (PIPG) using only RGB images from a calibrated camera. The novice first captures the patient using the camera on a mixed reality (MR) head-mounted display (HMD). An edge server then infers a patient-specific body-surface and skeleton model, with spatial smoothing across multiple views. Using bony landmarks from the predicted skeleton, we estimate the intercostal region and project the guidance back onto the reconstructed body surface. To validate the framework, we overlaid the reconstructed body mesh and the virtual probe pose guidance across multiple transthoracic echocardiography scan planes in situ and measured the quantitative placement error. Pilot experiments with healthy volunteers suggest that the proposed probe placement prediction and MR guidance yield consistent initial placement within anatomical variability acceptable for teleultrasound setup

摘要（中文）: 心脏和肺部超声在技术上要求很高，因为操作者必须识别患者特定的肋间声窗，然后通过调整探头的位置、旋转和压力在不同的成像平面之间切换，从而获取标准图像。当新手或机器人面临在没有专家现场协助的情况下，首先将探头放置在患者身上的困难任务时，这些挑战在远程超声中会被放大。我们提出了一种框架，仅使用来自校准相机的RGB图像，即可实现患者注册和基于解剖学信息的初始探头放置引导（PIPG）的自动化。新手首先使用混合现实（MR）头戴式显示器（HMD）上的相机捕捉患者。然后，边缘服务器推断出患者特定的体表和骨骼模型，并在多个视角上进行空间平滑处理。利用预测骨骼中的骨性标志，我们估计肋间区域，并将引导投射回重建的体表上。为了验证该框架，我们将重建的身体网格和虚拟探头姿态引导叠加到多个经胸超声心动图扫描平面上，并测量了定量的放置误差。对健康志愿者的初步实验表明，所提出的探头放置预测和MR引导可以在解剖学变异范围内实现一致的初始放置，这对于远程超声设置是可以接受的。

TLDR: This paper presents a framework for automated initial probe placement in transthoracic teleultrasound, using RGB images to infer a patient-specific body surface and skeleton model, and employing MR guidance to aid novice users. It addresses the challenge of remote ultrasound setup where expert in-person assistance is not available.

Authors: Yu Chung Lee, David G. Black, Ryan S. Yeung, Septimiu E. Salcudean

Context-dependent manifold learning: A neuromodulated constrained autoencoder approach

Abstract (English): Constrained autoencoders (cAE) provide a successful path towards interpretable dimensionality reduction by enforcing geometric structure on latent spaces. However, standard cAEs cannot adapt to varying physical parameters or environmental conditions without conflating these contextual shifts with the primary input. To address this, we integrated a neuromodulatory mechanism into the cAE framework to allow for context-dependent manifold learning. This paper introduces the Neuromodulated Constrained Autoencoder (NcAE), which adaptively parameterizes geometric constraints via gain and bias tuning conditioned on static contextual information. Experimental results on dynamical systems show that the NcAE accurately captures how manifold geometry varies across different regimes while maintaining rigorous projection properties. These results demonstrate that neuromodulation effectively decouples global contextual parameters from local manifold representations. This architecture provides a foundation for developing more flexible, physics-informed representations in systems subject to (non-stationary) environmental constraints.

摘要（中文）: 约束自编码器(cAE)通过在潜在空间强制执行几何结构，为可解释的降维提供了一条成功的途径。然而，标准cAEs无法适应变化的物理参数或环境条件，而不会将这些上下文偏移与主要输入混淆。为了解决这个问题，我们将一种神经调节机制集成到cAE框架中，以实现依赖于上下文的流形学习。本文介绍了一种神经调节约束自编码器(NcAE)，它通过基于静态上下文信息的增益和偏置调整，自适应地参数化几何约束。在动力系统上的实验结果表明，NcAE能够准确地捕捉流形几何如何在不同状态下变化，同时保持严格的投影特性。这些结果表明，神经调节有效地将全局上下文参数与局部流形表示解耦。该架构为在受（非平稳）环境约束的系统中开发更灵活、具有物理信息的表示奠定了基础。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Neuromodulated Constrained Autoencoder (NcAE) that adapts manifold geometry based on contextual information, decoupling global parameters from local representations. It is demonstrated on dynamical systems to capture manifold variations across different regimes.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种神经调节约束自编码器 (NcAE)，它可以根据上下文信息调整流形几何结构，从而将全局参数与局部表示分离。该方法已在动态系统上进行了演示，以捕获不同状态下的流形变化。

Authors: Jérôme Adriaens, Guillaume Drion, Pierre Sacré

Adapting Dijkstra for Buffers and Unlimited Transfers

Abstract (English): In recent years, RAPTOR based algorithms have been considered the state-of-the-art for path-finding with unlimited transfers without preprocessing. However, this status largely stems from the evolution of routing research, where Dijkstra-based solutions were superseded by timetable-based algorithms without a systematic comparison. In this work, we revisit classical Dijkstra-based approaches for public transit routing with unlimited transfers and demonstrate that Time-Dependent Dijkstra (TD-Dijkstra) outperforms MR. However, efficient TD-Dijkstra implementations rely on filtering dominated connections during preprocessing, which assumes passengers can always switch to a faster connection. We show that this filtering is unsound when stops have buffer times, as it cannot distinguish between seated passengers who may continue without waiting and transferring passengers who must respect the buffer. To address this limitation, we introduce Transfer Aware Dijkstra (TAD), a modification that scans entire trip sequences rather than individual edges, correctly handling buffer times while maintaining performance advantages over MR. Our experiments on London and Switzerland networks show that we can achieve a greater than two time speed-up over MR while producing optimal results on both networks with and without buffer times.

摘要（中文）: 近年来，基于RAPTOR的算法被认为是无预处理情况下无限次换乘路径搜索的最先进技术。然而，这一地位主要源于路由研究的演进，其中基于Dijkstra的解决方案被基于时间表的算法所取代，而没有进行系统的比较。在这项工作中，我们重新审视用于公共交通无限次换乘路径搜索的经典Dijkstra算法，并证明时间依赖Dijkstra算法（TD-Dijkstra）优于MR算法。然而，高效的TD-Dijkstra实现依赖于预处理期间过滤被支配的连接，这假设乘客总能切换到更快的连接。我们表明，当站点有缓冲时间时，这种过滤是不健全的，因为它无法区分可能无需等待即可继续的座位乘客和必须遵守缓冲时间的换乘乘客。为了解决这一局限性，我们引入了Transfer Aware Dijkstra（TAD），这是一种修改，它扫描整个行程序列而不是单个边，在正确处理缓冲时间的同时保持了优于MR的性能优势。我们在伦敦和瑞士网络上的实验表明，我们可以在两个网络上实现超过两倍于MR的速度提升，同时在有无缓冲时间的情况下产生最优结果。

TLDR: This paper revisits Dijkstra-based approaches for public transit routing, introducing a modification (TAD) to handle buffer times at stops and achieving faster performance than MR while guaranteeing optimal results. It's about more efficient path-finding algorithms, specifically for public transport.

简要说明: 本文重新审视了基于Dijkstra算法的公共交通路线规划方法，提出了一种名为TAD的改进方法，可以处理车站的缓冲时间，并且比MR算法更快，同时保证最优结果。 这是一个关于更有效的路径查找算法，专门用于公共交通的。

Authors: Denys Katkalo, Andrii Rohovyi, Toby Walsh

Portfolio of Solving Strategies in CEGAR-based Object Packing and Scheduling for Sequential 3D Printing

Abstract (English): Computing power that used to be available only in supercomputers decades ago especially their parallelism is currently available in standard personal computer CPUs even in CPUs for mobile telephones. We show how to effectively utilize the computing power of modern multi-core personal computer CPU to solve the complex combinatorial problem of object arrangement and scheduling for sequential 3D printing. We achieved this by parallelizing the existing CEGAR-SEQ algorithm that solves the sequential object arrangement and scheduling by expressing it as a linear arithmetic formula which is then solved by a technique inspired by counterexample guided abstraction refinement (CEGAR). The original CEGAR-SEQ algorithm uses an object arrangement strategy that places objects towards the center of the printing plate. We propose alternative object arrangement strategies such as placing objects towards a corner of the printing plate and scheduling objects according to their height. Our parallelization is done at the high-level where we execute the CEGAR-SEQ algorithm in parallel with a portfolio of object arrangement strategies, an algorithm is called Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ. Our experimental evaluation indicates that Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ outperforms the original CEGAR-SEQ. When a batch of objects for multiple printing plates is scheduled, Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ often uses fewer printing plates than CEGAR-SEQ.

摘要（中文）: 几十年前只能在超级计算机上获得的计算能力，特别是其并行性，现在在标准个人电脑 CPU 甚至移动电话 CPU 中都可以获得。我们展示了如何有效利用现代多核个人电脑 CPU 的计算能力来解决顺序 3D 打印中的对象排列和调度这一复杂的组合优化问题。我们通过并行化现有的 CEGAR-SEQ 算法来实现这一点，该算法通过将其表达为线性算术公式来解决顺序对象排列和调度问题，然后通过一种受反例引导抽象精化 (CEGAR) 启发的技巧来求解。原始的 CEGAR-SEQ 算法使用一种对象排列策略，将对象放置在打印板的中心位置。我们提出了替代的对象排列策略，例如将对象放置在打印板的角落附近，并根据对象的高度进行调度。我们的并行化是在高层进行的，即我们使用一系列对象排列策略并行执行 CEGAR-SEQ 算法，该算法被称为 Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ。我们的实验评估表明，Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ 优于原始的 CEGAR-SEQ。当调度多个打印板的一批对象时，Portfolio-CEGAR-SEQ 通常使用的打印板数量少于 CEGAR-SEQ。

TLDR: The paper introduces Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ, a parallelized algorithm for object arrangement and scheduling in 3D printing that leverages multiple object arrangement strategies to outperform the original CEGAR-SEQ algorithm.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为Porfolio-CEGAR-SEQ的并行算法，用于3D打印中的物体排列和调度，它利用多种物体排列策略，性能优于原有的CEGAR-SEQ算法。

Authors: Pavel Surynek

WORKSWORLD: A Domain for Integrated Numeric Planning and Scheduling of Distributed Pipelined Workflows

Abstract (English): This work pursues automated planning and scheduling of distributed data pipelines, or workflows. We develop a general workflow and resource graph representation that includes both data processing and sharing components with corresponding network interfaces for scheduling. Leveraging these graphs, we introduce WORKSWORLD, a new domain for numeric domain-independent planners designed for permanently scheduled workflows, like ingest pipelines. Our framework permits users to define data sources, available workflow components, and desired data destinations and formats without explicitly declaring the entire workflow graph as a goal. The planner solves a joint planning and scheduling problem, producing a plan that both builds the workflow graph and schedules its components on the resource graph. We empirically show that a state-of-the-art numeric planner running on commodity hardware with one hour of CPU time and 30GB of memory can solve linear-chain workflows of up to 14 components across eight sites.

摘要（中文）: 本研究致力于分布式数据流水线或工作流的自动化规划和调度。我们开发了一种通用的工作流和资源图表示方法，该方法包含了数据处理和共享组件，以及用于调度的相应网络接口。基于这些图，我们引入了WORKSWORLD，这是一种针对数值型领域无关规划器的新领域，专为永久调度的流水线工作流（例如摄取流水线）而设计。我们的框架允许用户定义数据源、可用的工作流组件，以及所需的数据目的地和格式，而无需显式声明整个工作流图作为目标。规划器解决一个联合规划和调度问题，生成一个既构建工作流图又在资源图上调度其组件的方案。我们通过实证表明，在普通硬件上运行的、具有一小时CPU时间和30GB内存的先进数值型规划器，可以解决跨越八个站点的、最多包含14个组件的线性链式工作流。

TLDR: The paper introduces WORKSWORLD, a new planning domain for numeric domain-independent planners aimed at automated planning and scheduling of distributed data pipelines, demonstrating scalability to linear-chain workflows with up to 14 components.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个名为WORKSWORLD的新规划领域，用于数字领域独立的规划器，旨在自动化规划和调度分布式数据管道。实验表明，该方法能够扩展到最多14个组件的线性链式工作流。

Authors: Taylor Paul, William Regli

Compiling Temporal Numeric Planning into Discrete PDDL+: Extended Version

Abstract (English): Since the introduction of the PDDL+ modeling language, it was known that temporal planning with durative actions (as in PDDL 2.1) could be compiled into PDDL+. However, no practical compilation was presented in the literature ever since. We present a practical compilation from temporal planning with durative actions into PDDL+, fully capturing the semantics and only assuming the non-self-overlapping of actions. Our compilation is polynomial, retains the plan length up to a constant factor and is experimentally shown to be of practical relevance for hard temporal numeric problems.

摘要（中文）: 自从 PDDL+ 建模语言问世以来，人们就知道可以使用 PDDL+ 将带有持续性动作的时序规划（如 PDDL 2.1 中）进行编译。然而，自此以后，文献中一直没有出现实际可行的编译方法。我们提出了一种将带有持续性动作的时序规划编译成 PDDL+ 的实际方法，该方法完全捕捉语义，并且只假设动作之间非自重叠。 我们的编译是多项式的，将计划长度保持在一个常数因子内，并且实验表明它对于困难的时序数值问题具有实际意义。

TLDR: This paper presents a practical, polynomial-time compilation method for converting temporal planning problems with durative actions into PDDL+, while preserving plan length up to a constant factor, demonstrating practical relevance for hard problems.

Flowcean - Model Learning for Cyber-Physical Systems

Abstract (English): Effective models of Cyber-Physical Systems (CPS) are crucial for their design and operation. Authors: Maximilian Schmidt, Swantje Plambeck, Markus Knitt, Hendrik Rose, Goerschwin Fey, Jan Christian Wieck, Stephan Balduin

AstroSplat: Physics-Based Gaussian Splatting for Rendering and Reconstruction of Small Celestial Bodies

Abstract (English): Image-based surface reconstruction and characterization are crucial for missions to small celestial bodies (e.g., asteroids), as it informs mission planning, navigation, and scientific analysis. Recent advances in Gaussian splatting enable high-fidelity neural scene representations but typically rely on a spherical harmonic intensity parameterization that is strictly appearance-based and does not explicitly model material properties or light-surface interactions. We introduce AstroSplat, a physics-based Gaussian splatting framework that integrates planetary reflectance models to improve the autonomous reconstruction and photometric characterization of small-body surfaces from in-situ imagery. The proposed framework is validated on real imagery taken by NASA's Dawn mission, where we demonstrate superior rendering performance and surface reconstruction accuracy compared to the typical spherical harmonic parameterization.

摘要（中文）: 基于图像的表面重建和表征对于小天体（如小行星）探测任务至关重要，因为它为任务规划、导航和科学分析提供信息。最近高斯溅射技术的进步实现了高保真度的神经场景表示，但通常依赖于球面谐波强度参数化，该参数化严格基于外观，并且没有明确地对材料特性或光-表面相互作用进行建模。我们介绍AstroSplat，一个基于物理的高斯溅射框架，它集成了行星反射率模型，以改进从小天体表面原位图像进行自主重建和光度表征。所提出的框架已在NASA黎明号任务拍摄的真实图像上进行了验证，结果表明，与典型的球面谐波参数化相比，我们获得了更卓越的渲染性能和表面重建精度。

TLDR: AstroSplat introduces a physics-based Gaussian splatting framework for reconstructing and characterizing small celestial bodies from in-situ imagery, improving upon existing methods by explicitly modeling material properties and light-surface interactions, demonstrating superior performance on NASA's Dawn mission data.

简要说明: AstroSplat 提出了一种基于物理的 Gaussian splatting 框架，用于从原位图像重建和表征小型天体，通过显式建模材料属性和光-表面相互作用，改进了现有方法，并在 NASA 的 Dawn 任务数据上展示了卓越的性能。

Preliminary analysis of RGB-NIR Image Registration techniques for off-road forestry environments

Abstract (English): RGB-NIR image registration plays an important role in sensor-fusion, image enhancement and off-road autonomy. In this work, we evaluate both classical and Deep Learning (DL) based image registration techniques to access their suitability for off-road forestry applications. Single-View Rolling-Shutter SfM

Abstract (English): Rolling-shutter (RS) cameras are ubiquitous, but RS SfM (structure-from-motion) has not been fully solved yet. Authors: Sofía Errázuriz Muñoz, Kim Kiehn, Petr Hruby, Kathlén Kohn

COTONET: A custom cotton detection algorithm based on YOLO11 for stage of growth cotton boll detection

Abstract (English): Cotton harvesting is a critical phase where cotton capsules are physically manipulated and can lead to fibre degradation. To maintain the highest quality, harvesting methods must emulate delicate manual grasping, to preserve cotton's intrinsic properties. Automating this process requires systems capable of recognising cotton capsules across various phenological stages. To address this challenge, we propose COTONET, an enhanced custom YOLO11 model tailored with attention mechanisms to improve the detection of difficult instances. The architecture incorporates gradients in non-learnable operations to enhance shape and feature extraction. Key architectural modifications include: the replacement of convolutional blocks with Squeeze-and-Exitation blocks, a redesigned backbone integrating attention mechanisms, and the substitution of standard upsampling operations for Content Aware Reassembly of Features (CARAFE). Additionally, we integrate Simple Attention Modules (SimAM) for primary feature aggregation and Parallel Hybrid Attention Mechanisms (PHAM) for channel-wise, spatial-wise and coordinate-wise attention in the downward neck path. This configuration offers increased flexibility and robustness for interpreting the complexity of cotton crop growth. COTONET aligns with small-to-medium YOLO models utilizing 7.6M parameters and 27.8 GFLOPS, making it suitable for low-resource edge computing and mobile robotics. COTONET outperforms the standard YOLO baselines, achieving a mAP50 of 81.1% and a mAP50-95 of 60.6%.

摘要（中文）: 棉花采摘是一个关键阶段，在此阶段棉花的棉铃会被物理性地操作，这可能导致纤维降解。为了保持最高质量，采摘方法必须模仿精细的手工抓取，以保留棉花的内在特性。该过程的自动化需要能够识别各种物候期棉铃的系统。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了COTONET，一个增强的定制YOLO11模型，该模型专门设计了注意力机制，以提高对难以检测的实例的检测能力。该架构在不可学习的操作中融入了梯度，以增强形状和特征提取。关键的架构修改包括：用Squeeze-and-Exitation块替换卷积块，重新设计的集成了注意力机制的主干网络，以及用内容感知特征重组（CARAFE）替换标准上采样操作。此外，我们集成了用于主要特征聚合的简单注意力模块（SimAM）和用于下行颈部路径中通道级、空间级和坐标级注意力的并行混合注意力机制（PHAM）。这种配置为解释棉花作物生长的复杂性提供了更大的灵活性和鲁棒性。COTONET与小型到中型的YOLO模型保持一致，利用760万个参数和27.8 GFLOPS，使其适合于低资源边缘计算和移动机器人应用。COTONET的性能优于标准YOLO基线，达到了81.1%的mAP50和60.6%的mAP50-95。

TLDR: The paper introduces COTONET, a modified YOLOv11 architecture incorporating attention mechanisms and other enhancements for improved cotton boll detection across various growth stages, suitable for low-resource edge computing.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了COTONET，一种改进的YOLOv11架构，结合了注意力机制和其他增强功能，以提高对不同生长阶段棉铃的检测能力，适用于低资源边缘计算。

Authors: Guillem González, Guillem Alenyà, Sergi Foix

Shadowless Projection Mapping for Tabletop Workspaces with Synthetic Aperture Projector

Abstract (English): Projection mapping (PM) enables augmented reality (AR) experiences without requiring users to wear head-mounted displays and supports multi-user interaction. It is regarded as a promising technology for a variety of applications in which users interact with content superimposed onto augmented objects in tabletop workspaces, including remote collaboration, healthcare, industrial design, urban planning, artwork creation, and office work. However, conventional PM systems often suffer from projection shadows when users occlude the light path. Prior approaches employing multiple distributed projectors can compensate for occlusion, but suffer from latency due to computational processing, degrading the user experience. In this research, we introduce a synthetic-aperture PM system that uses a significantly larger number of projectors, arranged densely in the environment, to achieve delay-free, shadowless projection for tabletop workspaces without requiring computational compensation. To address spatial resolution degradation caused by subpixel misalignment among overlaid projections, we develop and validate an offline blur compensation method whose computation time remains independent of the number of projectors. Furthermore, we demonstrate that our shadowless PM plays a critical role in achieving a fundamental goal of PM: altering material properties without evoking projection-like impression. Specifically, we define this perceptual impression as ``sense of projection (SoP)'' and establish a PM design framework to minimize the SoP based on user studies.

摘要（中文）: 投影映射（PM）能够实现增强现实（AR）体验，无需用户佩戴头戴式显示器，并支持多用户互动。它被认为是一项前景广阔的技术，适用于用户与叠加在桌面工作区中增强对象上的内容进行交互的各种应用，包括远程协作、医疗保健、工业设计、城市规划、艺术创作和办公工作。然而，传统的PM系统通常会在用户遮挡光路时受到投影阴影的影响。先前采用多个分布式投影仪的方法可以补偿遮挡，但由于计算处理而产生延迟，从而降低了用户体验。在本研究中，我们引入了一种合成孔径PM系统，该系统使用大量投影仪密集地排列在环境中，以实现无需计算补偿的桌面工作区无延迟、无阴影投影。为了解决叠加投影之间亚像素未对准引起的空间分辨率下降问题，我们开发并验证了一种离线模糊补偿方法，该方法的计算时间与投影仪的数量无关。此外，我们证明了我们的无阴影PM在实现PM的一个基本目标方面发挥着关键作用：在不引起类似投影的印象的情况下改变材料属性。具体来说，我们将这种感知印象定义为“投影感（SoP）”，并建立了一个基于用户研究的PM设计框架，以最大限度地减少SoP。

TLDR: This paper introduces a synthetic-aperture projection mapping system with many projectors to achieve shadowless projection and minimize the 'sense of projection' on tabletop workspaces, enhanced by an offline blur compensation method.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种合成孔径投影映射系统，该系统使用大量投影仪来实现无阴影投影，并最大限度地减少桌面工作空间中的“投影感”，并通过离线模糊补偿方法进行了增强。

Authors: Takahiro Okamoto, Masaki Takeuchi, Masataka Sawayama, Daisuke Iwai

High-Precision 6DOF Pose Estimation via Global Phase Retrieval in Fringe Projection Profilometry for 3D Mapping

Abstract (English): Digital fringe projection (DFP) enables micrometer-level 3D reconstruction, yet extending it to large-scale mapping remains challenging because six-degree-of-freedom pose estimation often cannot match the reconstruction's precision. Conventional iterative closest point (ICP) registration becomes inefficient on multi-million-point clouds and typically relies on downsampling or feature-based selection, which can reduce local detail and degrade pose precision. Drift-correction methods improve long-term consistency but do not resolve sampling sensitivity in dense DFP point clouds.We propose a high-precision pose estimation method that augments a moving DFP system with a fixed, intrinsically calibrated global projector. Using the global projector's phase-derived pixel constraints and a PnP-style reprojection objective, the method estimates the DFP system pose in a fixed reference frame without relying on deterministic feature extraction, and we experimentally demonstrate sampling invariance under coordinate-preserving subsampling. Experiments demonstrate sub-millimeter pose accuracy against a reference with quantified uncertainty bounds, high repeatability under aggressive subsampling, robust operation on homogeneous surfaces and low-overlap views, and reduced error accumulation when used to correct ICP-based trajectories. The method extends DFP toward accurate 3D mapping in quasi-static scenarios such as inspection and metrology, with the trade-off of time-multiplexed acquisition for the additional projector measurements.

摘要（中文）: 数字条纹投影(DFP)可实现微米级三维重建，然而将其扩展到大规模测绘仍具有挑战性，因为六自由度姿态估计往往无法与重建精度相匹配。传统的迭代最近点(ICP)配准在数百万点云上效率低下，通常依赖于降采样或基于特征的选择，这会降低局部细节并降低姿态精度。漂移校正方法可以提高长期一致性，但无法解决密集DFP点云中的采样敏感性。我们提出了一种高精度姿态估计方法，该方法利用一个固定的、经过内参标定的全局投影仪来增强移动的DFP系统。该方法使用全局投影仪的相位导出的像素约束以及类似PnP的重投影目标，在固定参考系中估计DFP系统姿态，而无需依赖确定性的特征提取。我们通过实验证明了在坐标保持的二次采样下的采样不变性。实验表明，针对具有量化不确定性边界的参考系，实现了亚毫米级的姿态精度；在激进的二次采样下具有很高的可重复性；在均匀表面和低重叠视图上具有稳健的操作性能；并且在用于校正基于ICP的轨迹时，减少了误差累积。该方法将DFP扩展到准静态场景（如检测和计量）中的精确3D测绘，其代价是用时分复用采集的方式获取额外的投影仪测量数据。

TLDR: The paper introduces a high-precision 6DOF pose estimation method for fringe projection profilometry by using a global projector, addressing the limitations of ICP in large-scale 3D mapping and enabling accurate 3D mapping in quasi-static scenarios.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种高精度的条纹投影轮廓术六自由度位姿估计方法，该方法使用全局投影仪，解决了ICP在大规模三维mapping中的局限性，并实现了在准静态场景下的精确三维mapping。
