Authors: Sehoon Tak, Keunhee Cho, Sangpil Kim, Jae-Sang Hyun

InstantHDR: Single-forward Gaussian Splatting for High Dynamic Range 3D Reconstruction

Abstract (English): High dynamic range (HDR) novel view synthesis (NVS) aims to reconstruct HDR scenes from multi-exposure low dynamic range (LDR) images. Existing HDR pipelines heavily rely on known camera poses, well-initialized dense point clouds, and time-consuming per-scene optimization. Current feed-forward alternatives overlook the HDR problem by assuming exposure-invariant appearance. To bridge this gap, we propose InstantHDR, a feed-forward network that reconstructs 3D HDR scenes from uncalibrated multi-exposure LDR collections in a single forward pass. Specifically, we design a geometry-guided appearance modeling for multi-exposure fusion, and a meta-network for generalizable scene-specific tone mapping. Due to the lack of HDR scene data, we build a pre-training dataset, called HDR-Pretrain, for generalizable feed-forward HDR models, featuring 168 Blender-rendered scenes, diverse lighting types, and multiple camera response functions. Comprehensive experiments show that our InstantHDR delivers comparable synthesis performance to the state-of-the-art optimization-based HDR methods while enjoying $\sim700\times$ and $\sim20\times$ reconstruction speed improvement with our single-forward and post-optimization settings. All code, models, and datasets will be released after the review process.

摘要（中文）: 高动态范围（HDR）新视角合成（NVS）旨在从多曝光低动态范围（LDR）图像中重建HDR场景。现有HDR流程严重依赖于已知的相机姿态、良好初始化的密集点云以及耗时的逐场景优化。目前的直接前馈替代方案通过假设曝光不变的外观，忽略了HDR问题。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出InstantHDR，一个直接前馈网络，可在单次前向传递中从未经校准的多曝光LDR图像集合中重建3D HDR场景。具体而言，我们设计了一种几何引导的外观建模用于多曝光融合，以及一个用于可泛化场景特定色调映射的元网络。由于缺乏HDR场景数据，我们构建了一个预训练数据集HDR-Pretrain，用于可泛化的直接前馈HDR模型，该数据集包含168个Blender渲染场景、多样化的照明类型以及多种相机响应函数。综合实验表明，我们的InstantHDR在提供与最先进的基于优化的HDR方法相当的合成性能的同时，通过我们的单次前向和后优化设置，实现了约$700\times$和约$20\times$的重建速度提升。所有代码、模型和数据集将在评审过程后发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces InstantHDR, a feed-forward network utilizing Gaussian splatting for fast HDR 3D reconstruction from multi-exposure LDR images, achieving comparable or superior performance to optimization-based methods with significantly improved speed.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了InstantHDR，一个使用高斯溅射的前馈网络，用于从多重曝光LDR图像中快速进行HDR 3D重建，与基于优化的方法相比，实现了可比或更优越的性能，并显著提高了速度。

Authors: Dingqiang Ye, Jiacong Xu, Jianglu Ping, Yuxiang Guo, Chao Fan, Vishal M. Patel

Bayesian Optimization of Partially Known Systems using Hybrid Models

Abstract (English): Bayesian optimization (BO) has gained attention as an efficient algorithm for black-box optimization of expensive-to-evaluate systems, where the BO algorithm iteratively queries the system and suggests new trials based on a probabilistic model fitted to previous samples. Still, the standard BO loop may require a prohibitively large number of experiments to converge to the optimum, especially for high-dimensional and nonlinear systems. We present a hybrid model-based BO formulation that combines the iterative Bayesian learning of BO with partially known mechanistic physical models. Instead of learning a direct mapping from inputs to the objective, we write all known equations for a physics-based model and infer expressions for variables missing equations using a probabilistic model, in our case, a Gaussian process (GP). The final formulation then includes the GP as a constraint in the hybrid model, thereby allowing other physics-based nonlinear and implicit model constraints. This hybrid model formulation yields a constrained, nonlinear stochastic program, which we discretize using the sample-average approximation. In an in-silico optimization of a single-stage distillation, the hybrid BO model based on mass conservation laws yields significantly better designs than a standard BO loop. Furthermore, the hybrid model converges in as few as one iteration, depending on the initial samples, whereas, the standard BO does not converge within 25 for any of the seeds. Overall, the proposed hybrid BO scheme presents a promising optimization method for partially known systems, leveraging the strengths of both mechanistic modeling and data-driven optimization.

摘要（中文）: 贝叶斯优化 (BO) 作为一种高效的黑盒优化算法，在昂贵评估系统的优化中受到了广泛关注。BO 算法迭代式地查询系统，并基于拟合先前样本的概率模型来建议新的试验。然而，标准的 BO 循环可能需要非常大量的实验才能收敛到最优解，尤其是在高维和非线性系统中。我们提出了一种混合模型驱动的 BO 方案，该方案将 BO 的迭代贝叶斯学习与部分已知的机理物理模型相结合。不同于学习从输入到目标的直接映射，我们为基于物理的模型编写所有已知的方程，并使用概率模型（在我们的案例中为高斯过程（GP））推断缺失方程的变量表达式。最终的公式将 GP 作为混合模型中的约束，从而允许其他的基于物理的非线性和隐式模型约束。这种混合模型公式产生了一个受约束的非线性随机规划，我们使用样本平均近似对其进行离散化。在单级蒸馏的计算机模拟优化中，基于质量守恒定律的混合 BO 模型比标准的 BO 循环产生明显更好的设计。此外，根据初始样本的不同，混合模型在少至一次迭代中即可收敛，而标准 BO 在任何种子下，25 次迭代内均不收敛。总而言之，所提出的混合 BO 方案为部分已知系统提供了一种有前景的优化方法，利用了机理建模和数据驱动优化的优势。

TLDR: This paper introduces a hybrid Bayesian Optimization (BO) approach that combines mechanistic physical models with Gaussian Processes to optimize partially known systems, demonstrating faster convergence and better designs compared to standard BO in a distillation optimization problem.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种混合贝叶斯优化(BO)方法，该方法将机械物理模型与高斯过程相结合，以优化部分已知系统。在蒸馏优化问题中，与标准BO相比，该方法表现出更快的收敛速度和更好的设计。

Authors: Eike Cramer, Luis Kutschat, Oliver Stollenwerk, Joel A. Paulson, Alexander Mitsos

Examining Users' Behavioural Intention to Use OpenClaw Through the Cognition--Affect--Conation Framework

Abstract (English): This study examines users' behavioural intention to use OpenClaw through the Cognition--Affect--Conation (CAC) framework. The research investigates how cognitive perceptions of the system influence affective responses and subsequently shape behavioural intention. Enabling factors include perceived personalisation, perceived intelligence, and relative advantage, while inhibiting factors include privacy concern, algorithmic opacity, and perceived risk. Survey data from 436 OpenClaw users were analysed using structural equation modelling. The results show that positive perceptions strengthen users' attitudes toward OpenClaw, which increase behavioural intention, whereas negative perceptions increase distrust and reduce intention to use the system. The study provides insights into the psychological mechanisms influencing the adoption of autonomous AI agents.

摘要（中文）: 本研究通过认知-情感-意动 (CAC) 框架，考察用户使用 OpenClaw 的行为意向。 该研究调查了系统认知感知如何影响情感反应，进而塑造行为意向。 促成因素包括感知到的个性化、感知到的智能和相对优势，而抑制因素包括隐私担忧、算法不透明性和感知到的风险。 使用结构方程模型分析了来自 436 位 OpenClaw 用户的调查数据。 结果表明，积极的感知增强了用户对 OpenClaw 的态度，从而增加了行为意向，而消极的感知则增加了不信任感，并降低了使用该系统的意向。 本研究深入了解了影响自主人工智能代理采用的心理机制。

TLDR: This paper uses the Cognition-Affect-Conation (CAC) framework to investigate the factors influencing user adoption of the OpenClaw autonomous AI agent, finding that positive perceptions increase adoption while negative perceptions decrease it.

简要说明: 该论文使用认知-情感-意动 (CAC) 框架来研究影响用户采用 OpenClaw 自主 AI 代理的因素，发现积极的认知会增加采用率，而消极的认知会降低采用率。

Authors: Yiran Du

Efficient Cross-View Localization in 6G Space-Air-Ground Integrated Network

Abstract (English): Recently, visual localization has become an important supplement to improve localization reliability, and cross-view approaches can greatly enhance coverage and adaptability. Meanwhile, future 6G will enable a globally covered mobile communication system, with a space-air-ground integrated network (SAGIN) serving as key supporting architecture. Inspired by this, we explore an integration of cross-view localization (CVL) with 6G SAGIN, thereby enhancing its performance in latency, energy consumption, and privacy protection. First, we provide a comprehensive review of CVL and SAGIN, highlighting their capabilities, integration opportunities, and potential applications. Benefiting from the fast and extensive image collection and transmission capabilities of the 6G SAGIN architecture, CVL achieves higher localization accuracy and faster processing speed. Then, we propose a split-inference framework for implementing CVL, which fully leverages the distributed communication and computing resources of the 6G SAGIN architecture. Subsequently, we conduct joint optimization of communication, computation, and confidentiality within the proposed split-inference framework, aiming to provide a paradigm and a direction for making CVL efficient. Experimental results validate the effectiveness of the proposed framework and provide solutions to the optimization problem. Finally, we discuss potential research directions for 6G SAGIN-enabled CVL.

摘要（中文）: 摘要： 近年来，视觉定位已成为提高定位可靠性的重要补充，而跨视角方法可以显著增强覆盖范围和适应性。同时，未来的6G将实现全球覆盖的移动通信系统，其中空天地一体化网络(SAGIN)是关键的支撑架构。受此启发，我们探索将跨视角定位(CVL)与6G SAGIN集成，从而提升其在延迟、能耗和隐私保护方面的性能。首先，我们对CVL和SAGIN进行了全面综述，强调了它们的能力、集成机会和潜在应用。受益于6G SAGIN架构快速且广泛的图像采集和传输能力，CVL实现了更高的定位精度和更快的处理速度。然后，我们提出了一种用于实现CVL的拆分推理框架，该框架充分利用了6G SAGIN架构的分布式通信和计算资源。随后，我们在所提出的拆分推理框架内进行通信、计算和保密性的联合优化，旨在为实现CVL的高效性提供一种范式和方向。实验结果验证了所提出框架的有效性，并为优化问题提供了解决方案。最后，我们讨论了6G SAGIN赋能的CVL的潜在研究方向。

TLDR: This paper explores integrating cross-view localization (CVL) with 6G space-air-ground integrated networks (SAGIN) to improve localization performance, proposing a split-inference framework and optimizing communication, computation, and confidentiality. The experimental results validate the framework's effectiveness.

简要说明: 本文探讨了将跨视角定位 (CVL) 与 6G 空天地一体化网络 (SAGIN) 相结合以提高定位性能，提出了一种分裂推理框架并优化了通信、计算和保密性。 实验结果验证了该框架的有效性。

Authors: Min Hao, Yanbing Xu, Maoqiang Wu, Jinglin Huang, Chen Shang, Jiacheng Wang, Ruichen Zhang, Jiawen Kang, Dusit Niyato, Zhu Han, Wei Ni

Hypercomplex Widely Linear Processing: Fundamentals for Quaternion Machine Learning

Abstract (English): Numerous attempts have been made to replicate the success of complex-valued algebra in engineering and science to other hypercomplex domains such as quaternions, tessarines, biquaternions, and octonions. Perhaps, none have matched the success of quaternions. The most useful feature of quaternions lies in their ability to model three-dimensional rotations which, in turn, have found various industrial applications such as in aeronautics and computergraphics. Recently, we have witnessed a renaissance of quaternions due to the rise of machine learning. To equip the reader to contribute to this emerging research area, this chapter lays down the foundation for: - augmented statistics for modelling quaternion-valued random processes, - widely linear models to exploit such advanced statistics, - quaternion calculus and algebra for algorithmic derivations, - mean square estimation for practical considerations. For ease of exposure, several examples are offered to facilitate the learning, understanding, and(hopefully) the adoption of this multidimensional domain.

摘要（中文）: 为了在工程和科学领域复制复数代数取得的成功，人们已尝试将此方法应用于其他超复数域，如四元数、泰萨林数、双四元数和八元数。然而，似乎没有一种能与四元数相媲美。四元数最实用的特性在于其能够模拟三维旋转，而这种能力又在航空和计算机图形学等各种工业应用中得到了应用。近年来，由于机器学习的兴起，我们见证了四元数的复兴。为使读者能够为这一新兴研究领域做出贡献，本章为以下内容奠定了基础：- 用于建模四元数值随机过程的增强统计方法，- 能够利用这些高级统计信息的广义线性模型，- 用于算法推导的四元数微积分和代数，- 用于实际考虑的均方估计。为了便于理解，提供了几个示例，以促进对这个多维领域的学习、理解和（希望）采用。

TLDR: This paper provides foundational knowledge for quaternion machine learning, covering augmented statistics, widely linear models, quaternion calculus, and mean square estimation, aiming to facilitate the adoption of this domain.

简要说明: 本文为四元数机器学习提供了基础知识，涵盖增强统计、广义线性模型、四元数微积分和均方估计，旨在促进该领域的应用。
